[001] CEB Flexi and Travel Fund
URL      : https://help.cebupacificair.com/article/ceb-flexi-and-travel-fund-123947
CATEGORY : Add-ons & Services
------------------------------------------------------------
# CEB Flexi and Travel Fund
Book your flight with CEB Flexi for more savings and flexibility in your travel plans. Cancel your flight for FREE and convert the value of your booking to a Travel Fund!

## Overview

### Description

## üìÜ CEB Flexi
Change of plans? No problem. With CEB Flexi, you can cancel your trip for free.
It allows you to cancel your booking and convert its value to a non-expiring Travel Fund.
- Cancelation is available up to two (2) hours before departure
- You can then use this Travel Fund to pay for your future travel plans!
Once you convert to Travel Fund, it will appear in your account within 24 hours.
General Guidelines:
- CEB Flexi only allows for free cancellation;It does not cover rebooking change fees.
- It does not cover rebooking change fees.
- You cannot add CEB Flexi after you've finished booking your flight;
- The price of CEB Flexi is based on your flight date, and on regulatory guidelines.
- If you purchased CEB Flexi without a MyCebuPacific account, and you intend to cancel your flight later on:Pleasesign up or log into your MyCebuPacific account first.Remember!An account is required to make booking changes.Check out ourhow-to guidesto know how to voluntarily cancel your flight and convert it to Travel Fund with CEB Flexi.
- Pleasesign up or log into your MyCebuPacific account first.
- Remember!An account is required to make booking changes.
- Check out ourhow-to guidesto know how to voluntarily cancel your flight and convert it to Travel Fund with CEB Flexi.

## ü™ô Travel Fund
Travel Fund is a non-expiring virtual wallet that you can use to pay for your future trips. It's available if:
- You purchased CEB Flexi and used it to cancel your flight, or;
- Your flight was disrupted (i.e. canceled or had a 1hr+ schedule change).How to Manage Your Disrupted Flight
- How to Manage Your Disrupted Flight
- Guest/s in the booking has a serious illness, or has died;Guest's immediate family member has died.
- Guest's immediate family member has died.
- AMyCebuPacific Accountis required to make booking changes;
- Once you convert to Travel Fund, it will appear in your MyCebuPacific account within 24 hours;
- The currency of your Travel Fund will depend on what currency you used when booking your flight.
- The Travel Fund can be split among guests in the same booking.With this, pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help you.
- With this, pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help you.
- ‚ùå The Travel Fund cannot be exchanged or converted to cash.
When you convert a booking to Travel Fund, it includes:
- Fares and taxes;
- All unused add-ons
- Admin and handling fees.
Conversion to Travel Fund does not include:
- Travel taxas this is refunded separately;
- Cost of CEB Flexi;
- Cost ofCEB TravelSure insuranceas this is refunded separately;
- Flight fees, such as the hold fee and cancel fee (if applicable).

### CEB Flexi

### Travel Fund

### Troubleshooting

# CEB Meals
Don‚Äôt go hungry on your flight, pre-order a meal now!

## Overview

### Description

## üç¥ CEB Meals
üçΩÔ∏è Need to satisfy your in-flight cravings? With the CEB Meals add-on, you can pre-order freshly cooked meals and snacks.
- You can pre-order your hot meals when youbook your flight, or;
- Through Manage Booking on theCebu Pacific appup to 24 hours before your flight.A MyCebuPacific account is required to buy or add CEB Meals.Sign upnow!
‚åõ Hot meals must be purchased 24 hours ahead, so we can prepare your meals fresh and ensure food safety.
Light snacks and drinks are available for purchase from our Fun Cafe on board on all flights but are subject to availability.
Learn more about our meal options here:Meal options
‚ö†Ô∏è Inflight meals (pre-ordered and buy-on-board) and merchandise are currentlynot available on all AirSWIFT (T6)-operated flights.
General Guidelines:
- Allergens may vary due to the available ingredients used.The actual meal served will have the final allergens on the label.
- The actual meal served will have the final allergens on the label.
- Drinking water is included with your CEB Meal order.Each pre-ordered meal comes with a free bottled water. Other beverages may also¬†be purchased in-flight.
- Each pre-ordered meal comes with a free bottled water. Other beverages may also¬†be purchased in-flight.
- For domestic and short-haul flights:You can order up to two (2) meals per guest, per flight.
- You can order up to two (2) meals per guest, per flight.
- For long-haul flights:You can order up to four (4)¬†meals per guest, per flight.Meals for long-haul flights are served 1h after take-off and 2h before landing.
- You can order up to four (4)¬†meals per guest, per flight.
- Meals for long-haul flights are served 1h after take-off and 2h before landing.

## Policies & Guides

### CEB Meals Policies

### Unserved CEB Meals
We're sorry for not serving your meal. Please chat with ourlive agents, available 24/7.

### Refunding CEB Meals

## ‚úã Voluntary cancelation
Please be reminded that pre-purchased CEB Meals arenon-cancelableandnon-refundable.
For more information, visit this¬†article:Rebooking or Canceling Your Flight

## üí° Carrying over / rebooking CEB Meals Add-on
Your CEB Meal Add-on should carry over to your new flight if:
- You rebooked, and your new flight is more than 24 hours away.
If your new flight is less than 24h away:
- Disrupted flights: You will be refunded the value of your meal
- Voluntary rebooking: Your CEB Meals will be forfeited

### How to pre-order a meal
Bo. Book a flight on the Cebu Pacific app
On. Once you reach the add-ons page, tap on "CEB Meals"
Se. Select your meals
Pr. Proceed to pay for your flight
Lo. Log into your MyCebuPacific account and tap "My Bookings"
Sc. Scroll down until you see your booking and tap "Manage"üí°: Can't see your booking? You'll need toadd it to your accountfirst.
Un. Under Modify flight, tap "Manage add-ons"
Se. Select your mealsüí° Make sure to do this at least 24 hours or more before your flight.
Pr. Proceed to pay

### Troubleshooting
Here are some common troubleshooting steps you can try:
| General troubleshooting
| üë§Are you logged in?

- Signing up for a MyCebuPacific Account
| üîç Can't find your booking?
| You may have to add the booking to your account. Follow these steps:Adding or Linking a Booking to Your Account
- Adding or Linking a Booking to Your Account
| üóÇÔ∏è Do you have a group or travel agency booking?
| Please contact your agent / coordinator directly to make changes. Learn more here:Online Travel Agency (OTA) Bookings
- Online Travel Agency (OTA) Bookings
| ‚úàÔ∏è Did you book on an unauthorized third-party platform?
| You may have difficulty managing your booking as these platforms may issue booking reference numbers not recognized by our system.If you encounter any issues, pleasechat with usto connect with a Live Agent who can verify your booking.Learn more here:Online Travel Agency (OTA) Bookings
- You may have difficulty managing your booking as these platforms may issue booking reference numbers not recognized by our system.
- If you encounter any issues, pleasechat with usto connect with a Live Agent who can verify your booking.
- Learn more here:Online Travel Agency (OTA) Bookings
| Issues with CEB Meals
| Was your CEB Meal not served?
| We're sorry to hear that. Please chat with ourlive agents, available 24/7.
| Is it less than 24 hours before your flight?
| You cannot add CEB Meals if your flight is less than 24 hours away.

### Description

You can purchase it when youbook a flight, or through Manage Booking on theCebu Pacific app.
| Seat class
| Benefits
| ‚ú® Premium
| Extra legroomSeat near exit & lavatoryPriority boarding (except for Macau, China, and Dubai)

- Seat near exit & lavatory
- Priority boarding (except for Macau, China, and Dubai)
| ‚ûï Standard Plus:
| Extra legroomSeat near exit & lavatory
| üü° Standard:
| Seat of your choice
If you didn't buy Seat Selector, don't worry:
- ‚úÖ Everyone with a ticket is guaranteed a seat on the aircraft.
- üé≤ You will be assigned a random seat at check-inIf you're traveling with multiple guests, there's a chance you won't be seated together.If you're traveling with children, we recommend buying your seats in advance üòä

# CEB Special Baggage
Got oversized items for your trip? We accept special baggage like sports equipment, surfboards, musical instruments, and oversized bags for check-in, for a fee. Learn more below.

## Overview

### Description
- CEB Special Baggage is available up to two (2) hours before your flight.To add CEB Special Baggage to your booking, manage your booking via theCebu Pacific app.A MyCebuPacific account is required to buy or add CEB Special Baggage.Sign upnow!
- To add CEB Special Baggage to your booking, manage your booking via theCebu Pacific app.A MyCebuPacific account is required to buy or add CEB Special Baggage.Sign upnow!
- A MyCebuPacific account is required to buy or add CEB Special Baggage.Sign upnow!
- Each guest is only allowed one (1) of each kind of special baggage, and with a weight of 20kg each.
- However, if a guest brings more than 20kg, they will need to pay an¬†excess baggage fee.Take note! Baggage can be increased to a maximum weight of 32kg.
- Take note! Baggage can be increased to a maximum weight of 32kg.
- CEB Special Baggage may not be available on Cebgo (DG) flights due to limited space.
üí°For instructions on adding regular baggage allowance to your booking, please visit theCEB Baggage Guidelines and Upgrade Optionsarticle.

# CEB TravelSure

- A MyCebuPacific account is required to buy or add CEB Travelsure via Manage Booking.Sign upnow!
- CEB TravelSure Insurance Add-on is currently available for flights in the following countries:PhilippinesAustraliaThailandVietnam
- Philippines
- Australia
- Thailand
- Vietnam
- In partnership with Chubb Travel Insurance, we provide extensive coveragefor your trip such as:Emergency medical treatment in case of accidents while traveling in the Philippines or AsiaPersonal accident insuranceFlight Cancellation up to Flight Cost (available for Thailand¬†and Vietnam only)Compensation for lost or damaged baggage (available for Philippines and Australia only)
- Emergency medical treatment in case of accidents while traveling in the Philippines or Asia
- Personal accident insurance
- Flight Cancellation up to Flight Cost (available for Thailand¬†and Vietnam only)
- Compensation for lost or damaged baggage (available for Philippines and Australia only)

# CEB Flexi and Travel Fund
Book your flight with CEB Flexi for more savings and flexibility in your travel plans. Cancel your flight for FREE and convert the value of your booking to a Travel Fund!

## Overview

### Description

## üìÜ CEB Flexi
Change of plans? No problem. With CEB Flexi, you can cancel your trip for free.
It allows you to cancel your booking and convert its value to a non-expiring Travel Fund.
- Cancelation is available up to two (2) hours before departure
- You can then use this Travel Fund to pay for your future travel plans!
Once you convert to Travel Fund, it will appear in your account within 24 hours.
General Guidelines:
- CEB Flexi only allows for free cancellation;It does not cover rebooking change fees.
- It does not cover rebooking change fees.
- You cannot add CEB Flexi after you've finished booking your flight;
- The price of CEB Flexi is based on your flight date, and on regulatory guidelines.
- If you purchased CEB Flexi without a MyCebuPacific account, and you intend to cancel your flight later on:Pleasesign up or log into your MyCebuPacific account first.Remember!An account is required to make booking changes.Check out ourhow-to guidesto know how to voluntarily cancel your flight and convert it to Travel Fund with CEB Flexi.
- Pleasesign up or log into your MyCebuPacific account first.
- Remember!An account is required to make booking changes.
- Check out ourhow-to guidesto know how to voluntarily cancel your flight and convert it to Travel Fund with CEB Flexi.

## ü™ô Travel Fund
Travel Fund is a non-expiring virtual wallet that you can use to pay for your future trips. It's available if:
- You purchased CEB Flexi and used it to cancel your flight, or;
- Your flight was disrupted (i.e. canceled or had a 1hr+ schedule change).How to Manage Your Disrupted Flight
- How to Manage Your Disrupted Flight
- Guest/s in the booking has a serious illness, or has died;Guest's immediate family member has died.
- Guest's immediate family member has died.
- AMyCebuPacific Accountis required to make booking changes;
- Once you convert to Travel Fund, it will appear in your MyCebuPacific account within 24 hours;
- The currency of your Travel Fund will depend on what currency you used when booking your flight.
- The Travel Fund can be split among guests in the same booking.With this, pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help you.
- With this, pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help you.
- ‚ùå The Travel Fund cannot be exchanged or converted to cash.
When you convert a booking to Travel Fund, it includes:
- Fares and taxes;
- All unused add-ons
- Admin and handling fees.
Conversion to Travel Fund does not include:
- Travel taxas this is refunded separately;
- Cost of CEB Flexi;
- Cost ofCEB TravelSure insuranceas this is refunded separately;
- Flight fees, such as the hold fee and cancel fee (if applicable).

## Policies & Guides

### Making Payments
üëØ Feel free to book for someone else! We recommend putting in their contact details so they can get updates about their flight.You may also use your Travel Fund to book for your family and friends. Learn more here:CEB Flexi and Travel Fund
- If your booking has an unpaid balance or amount due, you won't be able to board the flight.
- Please settle all balances or unpaid amounts before the day of flight or before checking in for your flight.
- Know how to pay for your amount due in ourhow-to guide.

| Unsettled amount
| Fee
| < 1,399 AED
| 100 AED
| > 1,400 AED
| 10% of unsettled amount
Lo. Log into your MyCebuPacific account and tap "My Bookings"
Sc. Scroll down until you see your booking with the Amount Due label and tap "Pay now"üí°: Can't see your booking? You'll need toadd it to your accountfirst.
Pr. Proceed to pay for your due balance
Ge. Get your confirmation and view your updated itinerary!
üí∑ The currency of the booking depends on the currency of your origin destination.
- For example: If the flight is departing from Manila, and arriving in Singapore, the currency will be in Philippine Peso.
With our Dynamic Conversion Currency (DCC) service, the currency can only be changed if you choose to pay with acredit card.
With this, you have two options:
- Currency based on the origin destination
- Currency based on the credit card's currencyFor example: If the credit card was issued in Singapore, you may opt to pay in Singapore dollars.

[014] Traveling with Service and Emotional Support Animals
URL      : https://help.cebupacificair.com/article/traveling-with-service-and-emotional-support-animals-121965
CATEGORY : Adding or Linking a Booking to Your Account
------------------------------------------------------------
# Traveling with Service and Emotional Support Animals
Cebu Pacific welcomes dogs onboard as either service animals or emotional support animals. No other animals are allowed in the cabin.

## Overview

### Description

## üê∂ What's the difference?
| Type
| Service Dog
| Trained to perform specific tasks for individuals with reduced mobilities (i.e., seeing eye / hearing dog).
| Emotional Support Dog
| Provides comfort and emotional stability to help ease anxiety and depression through companionship. Not task-trained.
General Guidelines:
- Make sure to declare that you'll be bringing your dog with you at the time of booking or via Manage Booking.
- Only one (1) dog is allowed per flight.

## ‚úàÔ∏èAccepted Flights
| Flight
| Service Dogs
| Emotional Support Dogs
| Cebu Pacific (5J)
| ‚úÖ accepted
| Cebgo (DG)
| AirSWIFT (T6)
| ‚ùå not yet accepted; coming soon!
Other household pets may be shipped viaCEB Cargoonly.

## üìã Travel Requirements
| 1.Document confirming the service dog has been trained
| 1.Document with letterhead from your medical doctor supporting the need for emotional support animal
| 2.Complete and up-to-date vaccination card of the dog
| 3. Shipping permit issued by the Bureau of Animal Industry - Department of Agriculture
| 3.Shipping permit issued by the Bureau of Animal Industry - Department of Agriculture

## üêæ Accessories &¬†Setup
- Service Dogs:Must be securelyleashedat all times; not required to wear a mouth-restraint device (i.e., muzzle, mouthguard, mouth cover, collar).
- Emotional Support Dogs:Allowed inside asoft carrierthat fits under the seat (approx. 8in x 8in x 14in).If inside a soft carrier, a leash and mouth-restraint device are not required.If outside a soft carrier, both a leash and a mouth‚Äërestraint device are required.
- If inside a soft carrier, a leash and mouth-restraint device are not required.
- If outside a soft carrier, both a leash and a mouth‚Äërestraint device are required.

## üí∫ Seating Guidelines
- Dogscannot occupy a seator be seated in theexit row.
- Must fit on your lap or within your legroom.
Recommended setup:
- Sit by the window with your dog between you and the window.
If your dog is too large:
- You may be moved to a seat with extra space (if available).
- If the flight is full, you may be rebooked to a later flight to accommodate you and your dog better.
- To guarantee space,purchase an extra seat.Chat with usso we can help you purchase an extra seat.

## üßº Hygiene & Comfort
- Service and emotional support dogs must wearpet diapersand sit onmoisture-absorbing material.
- Alternatively, provide a document stating your dogdoes not need to relieve itselfduring the flight.

## üåé Government Clearances
- All animals imported, transhipped, or exported to/fromSingaporerequire a validAnimal & Veterinary Service (AVS)license.
- For travel to/fromAustralia,refer to this articlefor Seeing Eye dog guidelines.

# Updating Your Guest or Contact Details
Made a typo? You can go to Manage Booking within 24 hours of booking to change either your First or your Last Name! You can also update your other contact and guest details up to 2 hours before your flight.

## Overview

### Description

## ‚úèÔ∏èUpdate Name
- ‚ö†Ô∏è You can update either yourFirst Name only, or yourLast Name only;
- ‚è≥ You can only make this change within 24 hours from the time of booking completion;
- ‚òùÔ∏èYou can only update this once.
If it's more than 24 hours since you made your booking:
- üí¨ Pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can validate your request;
- üìÑ Please prepare proof of the name correction, e.g., marriage certificate, or other supporting documents.
Special characters in your name:
- If your name has special characters (e.g., √±, √©, √º) please replace them with the regular letter instead (e.g., Ni√±a ‚û°Ô∏è Nina).
- For names with apostrophes or hyphens, you may replace them with a space (e.g., Mary-Jane‚û°Ô∏è Mary Jane, O'Connor ‚û°Ô∏è O Connor).
- If your boarding pass or itinerary shows your name without special characters, don't worry! Your booking is still valid.
Suffixes in your name:
- If your name has a suffix (Jr., Sr., III), proceed to enter the suffix in the "First Name" field.
- Enter your name exactly as it is shown in your valid ID.
General Guidelines:
- üë§ An account is required to make any booking changes.
- ‚ùå Booking isNOTtransferable to another guest.

## ‚úíÔ∏èUpdate Nationality/Passport, Birthday, Salutation, or Contact Number
You can update these details up to 2 hours before your flight, via Manage Booking.
- ‚è≥ This is only available up to 2 hours before your flight;
- ‚òùÔ∏è For nationality/passport, birthday, and salutation details, you can only update this once.
- ‚úåÔ∏è For your contact number, you can update this multiple times as necessary.
- Please approach the airport counters for assistance.
For OFWs, you can change or add your Overseas Employment Certificate (OEC) / MIAA Exemption Certificate (MEC) number even after completion of booking through the following channels:
- Chat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can validate your request.
- If you're at the airport, please approach theOverseas Workers Welfare Administration (OWWA) counter.
- Once you're at the counter, present any of these documents, OEC issued by the OWWA; OEC Balik Manggagawa Certificate; or MEC.

## üì© Update Email Address

## Overview

### Description
‚úàÔ∏è Cebu Pacific operates flights on theManila-Guangzhou-Manilaroute four times weekly via Ninoy Aquino International Airport Terminal 3. All flights arrive at and depart fromGuangzhou Baiyun International Airport (CAN) Terminal 1.
Please note thatstartingJanuary 22, 2026, all flights to and from Guangzhou Baiyun International Airport will be relocated from Terminal 1 toTerminal 3.

## Guide & Travel Requirements

### General Guidelines
Passport and visa
- Make sure your passport is valid for at least six months from your date of entry and has at least one blank page.

China Arrival Card
- Upon arrival in Guangzhou, foreign citizens will be required to fill up the China Arrival Card.This can be accomplished via electronic kiosks at the airport or in paper form issued by airport staff at the arrival area.
- This can be accomplished via electronic kiosks at the airport or in paper form issued by airport staff at the arrival area.
As per theCivil Aviation Administration of China (CAAC),only power banks with 3C certification are allowed for flights within China.
- Please be advised that only 3C-certified power banks are allowed on domestic flights within China.
- While this restriction applies for domestic flights or travelwithinChina, we still recommend carrying a 3C-certified power bank when entering the country.
- Check for the encircled "CCC" marking on your power bank.The logo should not be a sticker.
Learn more about power bank specifications here:Power Bank Limitations on Cebu Pacific Flights
- Follow the signs to proceed to the immigration counters.
- Present your passport and visa (if applicable), along with your China Arrival Card form (if you're a foreign citizen).

- If you have any items to declare, you must fill in the ‚ÄúBaggage Declaration Form for Incoming/Outgoing Passengers‚Äù from China Customs and choose the "Declaration Channel" (also named "Red Channel") for Customs clearance.
- Declare if you're carrying:Animals and plants (Including products made of animals and plants, microorganisms, biological products, human organs, blood products);Items worth CNY 5,000 or more for personal use;Items worth more than CNY 2,000 that a non-resident passenger intends to leave in China;Alcohol (containing more than 12% alcohol) with a volume of more than 1,500 ml; more than 400 cigarettes; more than 100 cigars; more than 500g of cut tobacco;More than CNY 20,000 in cash, or cash in a foreign currency which is equivalent to more than $5,000 USD;Separately-transported baggage, goods, samples of goods, advertisements;Any other items which are to be declared to Customs;If animal or plant quarantine is necessary, please obtain a certification of approval.

# Bangkok (Suvarnabhumi) Airport and Travel Guide
Plan your trip with this Bangkok Suvarnabhumi Airport travel guide, featuring Thailand's entry requirements, airport facilities, and essential travel tips.

## Overview

### Description
‚úàÔ∏è Cebu Pacific operates flights on theManila-Bangkok-Manilaroute twice daily via Ninoy Aquino International Airport Terminal 3, and on theClark-Bangkok-Clarkroute ten times weekly via Clark International Airport. All flights arrive at and depart from the Main Terminal of Bangkok Suvarnabhumi Airport (BKK).
Bangkok Suvarnabhumi Airport (BKK) is one of the busiest airports in Southeast Asia, serving as a major hub for international and domestic flights. It operates as asilent airport, meaning there are minimal public announcements to reduce noise pollution and create a more peaceful environment for travelers. Passengers are encouraged to rely on the flight information display screens (FIDS) located throughout the airport for updates on flight status, boarding gates, and other important information.

## Guide & Travel Requirements

### General Guidelines
Passport and visa
- Make sure your passport is valid for at least six months from your date of entry and has at least one blank page.
- Philippine passport holders can enter Thailand without a visa for stays no longer than 60 days.
- For non-Philippine passport holders, please check here if you'll need a visa:Cebu Pacific TravelDoc
Thailand Digital Arrival Card (TDAC)
- The TDAC is an online form that replaces the traditional paper-based arrival card for international travelers entering Thailand. This is free of charge and can be submitted within 3 days before entering Thailand.
- VisitThailand Digital Arrival Card (TDAC) articleto learn more.
- Followthe signs to the immigration counters and be prepared for possible random security checks.
- Present your passport and visa (if applicable) at the immigration counters.
- Travelers are encouraged to carry a digital or printed copy of the TDAC confirmation for reference upon arrival.
Claiming Baggage:
- After immigration, proceed to claim your baggage at the baggage claim area.
- Check the respective baggage carousel on the display screen for your flight.
- For any lost and found concerns, please emailbaggage.services@airportthai.co.th
- Use the green lane if you have nothing to declare, or the red lane if you have items to declare.
- For more information about Thailand's customs procedure for arriving passengers, visitThai Customs.
Philippine e-Travel Form:
- Anyone entering the Philippines, including guests on layover flights, must register for theeTraveland Customs Declarationwithin 72 hours before their flight.
- eTravel declaration is free of charge and is mandatory for travel to the Philippines.
- Arrive at the airport at least three (3) hours before your flight.Our airport counters close one (1) hour before departure.
- Our airport counters close one (1) hour before departure.
- Check the display screens to¬†find information aboutthe counters for your flight.
- Prepare your valid passport, booking confirmation or Itinerary Receipt, and visa (if applicable) for checking at the counters.
- Makeyour airport experience smoother and quicker by using Cebu Pacific‚Äôs self-service kiosks for check-in and bag tag printing. Simply prepare your booking reference number or barcode to retrieve your booking.

# Kaohsiung Airport and Travel Guide
Plan your trip with this Kaohsiung International Airport travel guide, featuring Taiwan's entry requirements, airport facilities, and essential travel tips.

## Overview

### Description
‚úàÔ∏è Cebu Pacific operates flights to and fromManila(Ninoy Aquino International Airport, Terminal 3) andKaohsiung(Kaohsiung International Airport, Terminal 1) 3x weekly.
Kaohsiung International Airport (KHH) is the primary air gateway to southern Taiwan. It features two modern terminals for international and domestic flights, equipped with amenities like duty-free shops, lounges, and free Wi-Fi. Additionally, it is well-connected by public transport and offers convenient options like MRT, taxis, and buses to downtown Kaohsiung.

## Guide & Travel Requirements

### General Guidelines
Passport and Visa:
- Make sure your passport is valid for at least six months from your date of entry and has at least one blank page.
- Taiwan extends its visa-free entry program to Philippine passport holders until July 31, 2026. As such, Filipinos can enter Taiwan without a visa for stays no longer than 14 days.
- For non-Philippine passport holders, please check here if you'll need a visa:Cebu Pacific TravelDoc.
Taiwan Arrival Card (TWAC):
- The Taiwan Arrival Card is a mandatory form that international travelers must complete before entering Taiwan. This is free of charge and can be submitted within three (3) days before entering Taiwan.Starting October 1, the form must be completed online as paper submissions will no longer be accepted.To learn more, check outTaiwan Arrival Card.
- Starting October 1, the form must be completed online as paper submissions will no longer be accepted.
- To learn more, check outTaiwan Arrival Card.
- Present your passport and visa (if applicable) at the immigration counters.
- Travelers are encouraged to carry a digital or printed copy of the TWAC confirmation, for reference upon arrival.
- Follow the "Arrivals" signs to proceed to the immigration counters.
Claiming Baggage:
- After immigration, proceed to claim your baggage at the baggage claim area.
- Check the respective baggage carousel on the display screen for your flight.
- For any lost and found concerns, pleasecontact886-7-8011060(Lost & Found Center, Kaohsiung Branch, Aviation Police Bureau).üì© You may also send an email toeyes@dns.apb.gov.tw.
- üì© You may also send an email toeyes@dns.apb.gov.tw.
- Passengers are strictly restricted from carrying the following products into Kaohsiung. Kindly make sure to remove all these items from your baggage:Fresh fruitsLive plants and their products(excluding those meeting the requirements stated in the Plant Protection and Quarantine Act)Live animals and their products, except for the following:Dried/processed aquatic productsDogs, cats, rabbits, and animal products meeting the requirements stated in the Statue for Prevention and Control of Infectious Animal Disease
- Fresh fruits
- Live plants and their products(excluding those meeting the requirements stated in the Plant Protection and Quarantine Act)
- Live animals and their products, except for the following:Dried/processed aquatic productsDogs, cats, rabbits, and animal products meeting the requirements stated in the Statue for Prevention and Control of Infectious Animal Disease
- Dried/processed aquatic products
- Dogs, cats, rabbits, and animal products meeting the requirements stated in the Statue for Prevention and Control of Infectious Animal Disease
- For more details on what you can bring and what to declare when entering Kaohsiung, check the official links below:Kaohsiung Customs - Agricultural or Cultural ProductsKaohsiung Customs - When to Declare
- Kaohsiung Customs - Agricultural or Cultural Products
- Kaohsiung Customs - When to Declare
Philippine e-Travel Form:
- Anyone entering the Philippines, including guests on layover flights, must register for theeTravel and Customs Declarationwithin 72 hours before their flight.
- eTravel declaration is free of charge and is mandatory for travel to the Philippines.
- Arrive at the airport at least three (3) hours before your flight.
- Our airport counters close one (1) hour before departure.
- Check the display screens to find information about the counters for your flight.
- Prepare your valid passport, booking confirmation or Itinerary Receipt, and visa (if applicable) for checking at the counters.
- Make your airport experience smoother and quicker by using Cebu Pacific‚Äôs self-service kiosks for check-in and bag tag printing. Simply prepare your booking reference number or barcode to retrieve your booking.
- Make sure to keep in mind your booking's baggage allowance.Learn more here:CEB Baggage Guidelines and Upgrade Options
- Learn more here:CEB Baggage Guidelines and Upgrade Options
Customs & Boarding:
- Passengers carryingany endangered species of wild fauna, flora and related produces shall submit Convention on International Trade in Endangered Species of Wild Fauna and Flora (CITES) certificates for customs declaration.
- Passengers exporting¬†live wildlife, or protected wildlife and products thereof referred to in Wildlife Conservation Act, approval documents issued by the Council of Agriculture Executive Yuan shall also be submitted.
- For more information on what you can bring and what to declare when exiting Kaohsiung, check the official links below:Kaohsiung Customs - Prohibited ArticlesKaohsiung Customs - When to Declare
- Kaohsiung Customs - Prohibited Articles
- Check your boarding pass and the nearest display screen to find the boarding gate number.
Passenger Rights:
- You have certain rights as an air passenger in case of flight disruptions.
- For more information, please visit the following articles:How to Manage Your Disrupted FlightDelays and Cancellations at the AirportPassenger Rights & Airline Policies
- How to Manage Your Disrupted Flight
- Delays and Cancellations at the Airport
- Passenger Rights & Airline Policies
- In the event of flight disruptions, passengers will be notified through various communication channels, including ground announcements and printed or digital signages.
- We also encourage passengers to monitor their email for important updates from Cebu Pacific.
Exiting the Airport:
- If your flight is disrupted after immigration and customs clearance, you may be allowed to exit Kaohsiung International Airport.
- Please be advised that any Duty-Free items must be refunded prior to exiting the airport.

Wr. Written parental consent attested by the Punong Barangay (if no parents, consent shall be made by the grandparents or eldest¬†sibling)
Id. Identification Card of the minor (original and photocopy)
Id. Identification Card of the authorized person who will accompany the child in his travels (original and photocopy).
If a child/minor is traveling with both or any of their parents,there is no need to secure a permitas long as there is a document to¬†prove the minor's relations such as:
Bi. Birth Certificate
Va. Valid IDs

- You have certain rights as an air passenger in case of flight disruptions.

[055] Airport Baggage Guidelines

------------------------------------------------------------
# Airport Baggage Guidelines
If you weren't able to buy baggage allowance ahead of time, or exceed the maximum weights or dimensions, you may be charged additional fees at the airport.

## Overview

### Description
To avoid high airport baggage fees,pre-purchase your CEB baggage allowance online. Learn more:CEB Baggage Guidelines and Upgrade Options
üí°You‚Äôll be charged an airport baggage fee if:
- You didn‚Äôt buy your checked baggage allowance online.
- You exceed the number of allowed baggage pieces.
- Your bag exceeds size or weight limits.
‚ö†Ô∏èExcess Baggage Fee
- Chargedper kiloover your allowance.
- Example: If you bought 20kg but check in 23kg, you‚Äôll pay for 3kg extra.
- No single bag can exceed 32kg.
üëúGate Baggage Fee
- Charged if yourhand-carry exceeds the allowed limit of 7kgs.
- Fees vary by booking date and regulations.
‚úÖAvoid extra fees by:
- Buying the right baggage allowance in advance.
- Keeping bags within size and weight limits.

# Guidelines for Connecting Flights
A quick guide to managing your connecting flights ‚Äî from check-in to baggage claim ‚Äî with special procedures for the Philippines and Australia, plus what to do if you miss any leg of your journey.

## Overview

### Description

### üì±Check-in and Boarding Passes
Before arriving at the airport, make sure tocheck in online!
If you can't check in online, you can check in at our regular airport counters instead.
- For connecting flights on the same booking,you should already receive two (2) boarding passes at your initial check-in.However, if your final destination is Australia(e.g., DVO‚ÄìMNL‚ÄìSYD), you still need to go to the check-in counter at Ninoy Aquino International Airport Terminal 3 (NAIA T3) to:Get your connecting flight's boarding pass; andGo through baggage screening.
- However, if your final destination is Australia(e.g., DVO‚ÄìMNL‚ÄìSYD), you still need to go to the check-in counter at Ninoy Aquino International Airport Terminal 3 (NAIA T3) to:Get your connecting flight's boarding pass; andGo through baggage screening.
- Get your connecting flight's boarding pass; and
- Go through baggage screening.
- For flights on separate bookings or with different airlines, you will need to check in again at the layover airport to obtain your boarding pass for the connecting flight.If you are connecting through a country that requires a visa, please ensure you have the necessary visa for that country. Failure to present a valid visa may result in denied boarding or entry.
- If you are connecting through a country that requires a visa, please ensure you have the necessary visa for that country. Failure to present a valid visa may result in denied boarding or entry.

## üß≥Baggage Check-in and Transfer
After your initial check-in, you can drop your baggage via:
- Self bag drop kiosks (for NAIA Terminal¬†3 only); or
- Regular bag drop counters
For flights on the same booking, your baggage (if any) will be checked through to your final destination ‚Äî except when entering the Philippines.
If you have a connecting flight from an international origin entering the Philippines as final destination (e.g., NRT‚ÄìMNL‚ÄìDGT), youmust:
Cl. Claim your baggageat your layover airport (e.g., MNL).
Cl. Clear Customswith your baggage.
Pr. Proceed to the Transfer Desknear Customs to endorse your baggage ‚Äî no need to check in again.
Go. Go to the pre-departure areafor your next flight.
Even if your connecting flights are on the same booking, these steps are required when entering the Philippines.
For flights on separate bookings, you need to collect your baggage at the layover / second airport and re-check it for the next flight.

## üß≥Security and Screening
For flights entering or exiting the Philippines, you need to:
- Register your flight viaeTravelwithin 72 hours (3 days) before departure, then save the QR code generated at the end of the form.
- Go through immigration screening.If your connecting flight is on Domestic‚ÄìDomestic‚ÄìInternational route, your immigration screening will be at the layover / second airport.
- If your connecting flight is on Domestic‚ÄìDomestic‚ÄìInternational route, your immigration screening will be at the layover / second airport.

# Lost, Damaged, or Delayed Baggage
What to do and where to reach out to if your baggage gets damaged, missing, or lost

## Overview

### Description

## üß≥ General Guidelines
The policies below apply tochecked baggageonly.
- If you lost/left items in the aircraft:Immediately report it to any Cebu Pacific ground staff,orchat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help.
- Immediately report it to any Cebu Pacific ground staff,
- orchat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help.

- Contact the airport‚ÄôsLost & Found officedirectly.
If your checked baggage was damaged, or did not arrive at your destination airport:
- Do not leave the airport;
- Immediately report it to any Cebu Pacific ground staff;
- Our staff will assist you in filing a Property Irregularity Report (PIR).

## ü©π Damaged Baggage
If yourchecked baggagearrived with a cracked surface or missing handle and/or wheels:
- We will assess if the damage exceeds¬†regular wear and tear;
- If so, we will provide compensation based on Philippine Air Passenger Bill of Rights or the Montreal Convention.

## üõÖ Missing / Delayed Baggage
If yourchecked baggagedid not arrive with you at the destination airport, please report it immediately.
While we locate your baggage, we will also provide you with the following delay compensation:
- üíµ Php2,000 for every 24 hours of delay
- üí≥If checked baggage is not delivered within 24 hours, the applicable baggage fees will be refunded.
We will notify you of the total compensation within 7 days of reporting.

## üîç Lost Baggage
If yourchecked baggageisn't found within 7 days of your arrival, we will consider your baggage lost.
We will compensate you with the value of the lost baggage, along with the delay compensation mentioned above.

## FAQ

### Other Policies
üß≥ Damaged or Missing Baggage?
If your checked baggage is damaged or missing,immediately report it to any Cebu Pacific staff while still at the airport. Our team will assist you in filing aProperty Irregularity Report (PIR).
üìåImportant:PIRs can only be filedwithin the airport premisesfor proper validation. Once you leave the airport, we can no longer accommodate PIR filing.
‚úÖSave your PIR Numberfor reference.
üì© We‚Äôll keep you updated on your baggage status via the email and/or mobile number you provided.
‚è≥ If you don‚Äôt receive an update within 24 hours, please reach out to us via chat on our app or website.
- Pick up the baggage from the destination airport; or
- Arrange for delivery to your registered address.
If your baggage is mistakenly claimed by another passenger and has been recovered, you need to pick up the recovered baggage at the airport.
If you mistakenly claimed someone else's baggage, please go back to the airport and inform any of the Cebu Pacific ground staff.

# CEB Baggage Guidelines and Upgrade Options
Bringing home extra pasalubong, or planning out your OOTDs?   If you need to bring more things, you can add CEB Baggage and CEB Special Baggage to your booking. It's available through Manage Booking up to 2 hours before your flight!

## Overview

### Description

## üß≥Checked baggage allowance
Checked baggage allowance is only included in our GO Easy and GO Flexi fare bundles:
| Fare Bundle
| Checked baggage allowance
| GO Basic
| ‚ùå None(Available as Add-on)
| GO Easy
| ‚úÖ 1 piece, 20kg allowance(Size limit: 39x39x39in)
| GO Flexi
For every 20kg of prepaid baggage allowance, you are entitled to bring one (1) piece of checked baggage.

## ‚ûïBaggage Upgrade and Extra Piece Purchase
- If you need toincrease the weight of your 20kg checked baggage, you may upgrade by 4kg, 8kg, or up to 12kg.Please note that upgrading the weight does not change the number of pieces allowed.
- Please note that upgrading the weight does not change the number of pieces allowed.
- If you need toincrease the number of pieces of your checked baggage, you can purchase a maximum of three (3) pieces online, with each piece having a base weight of 20kg.Should you require more than three pieces, additional baggage can be purchased at the airport.This does not apply to flights departingBangkok (BKK)andDon Mueang (DMK), where a temporary baggage policy limits airport purchases to two (2) pieces only.
- Should you require more than three pieces, additional baggage can be purchased at the airport.This does not apply to flights departingBangkok (BKK)andDon Mueang (DMK), where a temporary baggage policy limits airport purchases to two (2) pieces only.
- This does not apply to flights departingBangkok (BKK)andDon Mueang (DMK), where a temporary baggage policy limits airport purchases to two (2) pieces only.
- üí° If you need to bring larger or specialized items, consider gettingCEB Special Baggage Add-on.

## üëú Hand-carry allowance
| Hand-carry allowance
| ‚úÖ 1 piece for overhead binand 1 piece for under the seat, 7kg allowance(Size limit: 22inx 14in x 10in for baggage in the overhead bin and8in x 8in x 14in for baggage under the seat)

- Backpack or laptop/camera bag
- Sling bag, handbag, shoulder bag or small purse

# Passenger Rights and Airline Policies
Is your flight disrupted? Know your rights as an air passenger!

## Overview

### Description
- Cebu Pacific aims to keep passengers informed, especially when there are flight changes, so you can make alternative plans.

- To ensure passenger's welfare is taken care of whenever there are flight changes, Cebu Pacific will provide options based on the Philippine Air Passenger Bill of Rights.

### Description

- Declare the amount when filling your eTravel details
- For PH currency, secure authorization from the Bangko Sentral ng Pilipinas
Non-declaration or false declaration shall be subject to confiscation and/or legal action.
Before arriving at the airport, make sure to check in online!
If you can't check in online, you can line up at the regular airport counters.

[065] How to Manage Your Disrupted Flight

CATEGORY : Bangkok (Don Mueang) Airport and Travel Guide
------------------------------------------------------------
# How to Manage Your Disrupted Flight
Manage disrupted flights anywhere ‚Äî no need to visit the airport!

## Overview

### Description

## General Guidelines
While we continuously work to ensure your flight departs and arrives on time, on-the-spot delays or cancelations may occur due to environmental, operational or technical reasons.
- Affected passengers will be notified by Cebu Pacific frontline team, email, and/or text message.

# Thailand Introduces Digital Arrival Card for Foreigners
Starting May 1, 2025, all foreign guests must complete the Thailand Digital Arrival Card (TDAC) before entering the country.

## Overview

### Description
This requirement doesnotapply to the following:
- Thai nationals;
- Travelers transiting or transferring through Thailand without passing through immigration control; and
- Travelers entering using a Border Pass.
Foreign guests can complete and submit the TDAConlineor by scanning the QR code below.
The form requires information such as:
- Personal and Passport Information
- Flight and Accommodation Information
- Health Declaration
There is no fee for submitting the TDAC, and travelers are encouraged to carry a digital or printed copy of the TDAC confirmation for reference upon arrival.

# Passenger Rights and Airline Policies

### Description
- Cebu Pacific aims to keep passengers informed, especially when there are flight changes, so you can make alternative plans.
- If schedule changes or disruptions happen, notifications may be provided through email, text message, Cebu Pacific's social networking sites, Cebu Pacific website, airport screens, and/or airport or onboard announcements.

## üìú Provision of Options
- To ensure passenger's welfare is taken care of whenever there are flight changes, Cebu Pacific will provide options based on the Philippine Air Passenger Bill of Rights.

# Payment and Receipt Concerns
Learn more about the Itinerary Receipt, Invoice and your options when paying for flights and add-ons.

## Overview

### Description

## üíµ Accepted Forms of Payment
You can pay for your flight or add-ons with the following options:

## ‚úàÔ∏è Go Rewards
You can redeem or use your Go Rewards points in the Cebu Pacific app or website.
- Learn more here:How to Earn and Redeem Go Rewards Points

## ü™ô Travel Fund
The Travel Fund is a virtual wallet and can be used to pay for flights and add-ons.
- Learn more here:CEB Flexi and Travel Fund

## üí≥ Credit / Debit Card
Cebu Pacific accepts the following card types:
Vi. Visa
Ma. MasterCard
Am. American Express (AMEX)
JC. JCB

## üëõ e-Wallet
Cebu Pacific accepts the following e-Wallets:
GC. GCash
Gr. GrabPay
Ma. Maya
Pa. PayPal
- Make sure you have an existing and verified account to use the e-Wallet option.
- GrabPay, GCash, and Maya only accept payments in Philippine Peso (PHP).Your booking total will be converted to PHP, and you'll be charged with the converted amount.
- Your booking total will be converted to PHP, and you'll be charged with the converted amount.

## üí° Other payment options
Our payment center option is currently unavailable. We currently do not support other payment methods other than those listed above.

## Policies & Guides

### Making Payments
üëØ Feel free to book for someone else! We recommend putting in their contact details so they can get updates about their flight.You may also use your Travel Fund to book for your family and friends. Learn more here:CEB Flexi and Travel Fund
- If your booking has an unpaid balance or amount due, you won't be able to board the flight.
- Please settle all balances or unpaid amounts before the day of flight or before checking in for your flight.
- Know how to pay for your amount due in ourhow-to guide.
üí° For guests on flights exiting Dubai,you may be charged a fee at the airport counters if your booking still has an unsettled balance.The following fees will apply:
| Unsettled amount
| Fee
| < 1,399 AED
| 100 AED
| > 1,400 AED
| 10% of unsettled amount
Lo. Log into your MyCebuPacific account and tap "My Bookings"
Sc. Scroll down until you see your booking with the Amount Due label and tap "Pay now"üí°: Can't see your booking? You'll need toadd it to your accountfirst.
Pr. Proceed to pay for your due balance
Ge. Get your confirmation and view your updated itinerary!
üí∑ The currency of the booking depends on the currency of your origin destination.
- For example: If the flight is departing from Manila, and arriving in Singapore, the currency will be in Philippine Peso.
With our Dynamic Conversion Currency (DCC) service, the currency can only be changed if you choose to pay with acredit card.
With this, you have two options:
- Currency based on the origin destination
- Currency based on the credit card's currencyFor example: If the credit card was issued in Singapore, you may opt to pay in Singapore dollars.
- For example: If the credit card was issued in Singapore, you may opt to pay in Singapore dollars.

[073] CEB Flexi and Travel Fund
URL      : https://help.cebupacificair.com/article/123947
CATEGORY : Booking Flights with Cebu Pacific
------------------------------------------------------------
# CEB Flexi and Travel Fund
Book your flight with CEB Flexi for more savings and flexibility in your travel plans. Cancel your flight for FREE and convert the value of your booking to a Travel Fund!

## Overview

### Description

## üìÜ CEB Flexi
Change of plans? No problem. With CEB Flexi, you can cancel your trip for free.
It allows you to cancel your booking and convert its value to a non-expiring Travel Fund.
- Cancelation is available up to two (2) hours before departure
- You can then use this Travel Fund to pay for your future travel plans!
Once you convert to Travel Fund, it will appear in your account within 24 hours.
General Guidelines:
- CEB Flexi only allows for free cancellation;It does not cover rebooking change fees.
- It does not cover rebooking change fees.
- You cannot add CEB Flexi after you've finished booking your flight;
- The price of CEB Flexi is based on your flight date, and on regulatory guidelines.
- If you purchased CEB Flexi without a MyCebuPacific account, and you intend to cancel your flight later on:Pleasesign up or log into your MyCebuPacific account first.Remember!An account is required to make booking changes.Check out ourhow-to guidesto know how to voluntarily cancel your flight and convert it to Travel Fund with CEB Flexi.
- Pleasesign up or log into your MyCebuPacific account first.
- Remember!An account is required to make booking changes.
- Check out ourhow-to guidesto know how to voluntarily cancel your flight and convert it to Travel Fund with CEB Flexi.

## ü™ô Travel Fund
Travel Fund is a non-expiring virtual wallet that you can use to pay for your future trips. It's available if:
- You purchased CEB Flexi and used it to cancel your flight, or;
- Your flight was disrupted (i.e. canceled or had a 1hr+ schedule change).How to Manage Your Disrupted Flight
- How to Manage Your Disrupted Flight
- Guest/s in the booking has a serious illness, or has died;Guest's immediate family member has died.
- Guest's immediate family member has died.
- AMyCebuPacific Accountis required to make booking changes;
- Once you convert to Travel Fund, it will appear in your MyCebuPacific account within 24 hours;
- The currency of your Travel Fund will depend on what currency you used when booking your flight.
- The Travel Fund can be split among guests in the same booking.With this, pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help you.
- With this, pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help you.
- ‚ùå The Travel Fund cannot be exchanged or converted to cash.
When you convert a booking to Travel Fund, it includes:
- Fares and taxes;
- All unused add-ons
- Admin and handling fees.
Conversion to Travel Fund does not include:
- Travel taxas this is refunded separately;
- Cost of CEB Flexi;
- Cost ofCEB TravelSure insuranceas this is refunded separately;
- Flight fees, such as the hold fee and cancel fee (if applicable).

### Travel Fund

# Cebu Pacific Fare Bundles
Check out the ways you can save through Cebu Pacific's Fare Bundles!

## Overview

### Description

## ‚úàÔ∏è Fare Rules
üí° With a fare bundle, you can purchase our add-ons at a lower price compared to when it's purchased individually.
Cebu Pacific offers the following fare bundles. Click each listed item to learn more about our specific policies:
| Fare Bundle
| Inclusions
| GO Basic
| Voluntary cancellation:Not allowed, available withCEB Flexi add-on.Baggage allowance:7kg hand-carry only.Seat Selector:Random seat assigned at check-in.Voluntary rebooking:Allowed but subject to change fees and fare differences.Name correction:First Name or Last Name only. Must be changed within 24 hours of booking.No Show:Fares and fees will be forfeited or considered flown
| GO Easy
| Voluntary cancellation:Not allowed, available withCEB Flexi add-on.Baggage allowance:7kg hand-carry + 1pc 20kg checked baggage.Seat Selector:You may choose your preferred Standard Seat.Voluntary rebooking:Allowed but subject to change fees and fare differences.Name correction:First Name or Last Name only. Must be changed within 24 hours of booking.No Show:Fares and fees will be forfeited or considered flown.
General Guidelines:
- Selection of a fare bundle can only be done at the time of booking.
- The bundle will apply to all guests in the booking.
- When booking a round-trip flight, the bundle will apply to both your departure and return flights.
- You cannot switch your bundle to another (e.g. from GO Basic to GO Easy).
- üíº You can add or upgrade your baggage allowance after you select a fare bundle.
- üç¥ Other add-ons, such asCEB MealsandCEB Sports Equipment, are also available after you select a fare bundle.

[076] Traveling with Infants or Minors
URL      : https://help.cebupacificair.com/article/124189
CATEGORY : Booking Flights with Cebu Pacific
------------------------------------------------------------
# Traveling with Infants or Minors
Learn about age-specific travel rules, seat options, and required documents for infants and minors flying with Cebu Pacific to ensure a safe and smooth journey.

## Overview

### Description

## üë∂ Infant or below 2 years old
AnInfant Feewill be applied to guests traveling with an infant due to the special assistance required. Guests have the following options:
- Infant without seat:The infant will sit on the adult's lap.No baggage allowance will be given for infants on lap.
- The infant will sit on the adult's lap.
- No baggage allowance will be given for infants on lap.
- Infant with seat:The infant will occupy their own seat next to the parent/guardian's‚Äîcharged at the lowest available fare.The infant will have their own hand-carry baggage allowance. They can also purchase up to three (3) pieces of checked baggage.Infants with seat are required to have a Child Restraint System (CRS) that conforms to Federal Motor Vehicle Safety Standards (FMVSS) or certified by the Civil Aviation Authority (CAA).
- The infant will occupy their own seat next to the parent/guardian's‚Äîcharged at the lowest available fare.
- The infant will have their own hand-carry baggage allowance. They can also purchase up to three (3) pieces of checked baggage.
- Infants with seat are required to have a Child Restraint System (CRS) that conforms to Federal Motor Vehicle Safety Standards (FMVSS) or certified by the Civil Aviation Authority (CAA).
- For their safety, infants below 8 days old will not be accepted for carriage.
- Infants can only travel if accompanied by an adult aged 18 years and above. Only one (1) infant is allowed per adult passenger.
- Guests traveling with infants may present the infant's physical passport, birth certificate, or baby book as identification during check-in.
If you already booked a flight but weren't able to add the infant to your booking, visit this article:Adding an Infant to Your Booking

## üë∂Ages 2 to 6 years
Children below 7 years old are not allowed to travel alone. They may only be accepted if they are accompanied by a person at least 18 years old.
Please present a valid ID of the the traveling child at the airport.
- A birth certificate may be accepted for children without a school ID.
- Parents or guardians may be asked to submit additional identity verification at the check-in counter.
If a minor is traveling with both or any of their parents,there is no need to secure a permit¬†as long as there is a document to¬†prove the minor's relations such as:
Bi. Birth CertificateValid IDs
Bi. Birth Certificate
Va. Valid IDs

## üë∂Ages 7 to 11 years
Children aged 7 to 11 years are allowed to travel alone ondomestic flights only‚Äî they are not allowed to travel unaccompanied on international flights.
Requirements for minors traveling alone on domestic flights:
- Accomplished Unaccompanied Minor Form and paid Unaccompanied Minor Handling Fee
- ID of a parent/guardian accompanying the minor on departure
- ID of parent/guardian picking up the minor on arrival
- ID of traveling child
- Paid Unaccompanied Minor Handling Fee
- Confirmed flight segments
Learn more here:Unaccompanied Minor Requirements

## üë∂Ages 12 to 17 years
Young passengers aged 12 to 17 years are allowed to travel alone.
- Passengers below 18 years old traveling from Davaomust present Travel Permit issued by the City Social Welfare and Development Office (CSWDO)¬† or by the Special Office for Children's Concerns (SOCC) at check-in.
- Filipino passengers aged 12 to 17 yearstraveling alone to international destinationsmust present Travel Clearance issued by the Department of Social Welfare and Development (DSWD).
- Foreign passengers below 15 years old entering the Philippinesmust secure a Waiver of Exclusion Ground (WEG) from the Bureau of Immigration.

## FAQ

### FAQs
Fordomestic flights except from Davao, no special documents are needed as long as the accompanying adult is at least 18 years old. As with usual requirements for all passengers, the minor and accompanying adult will still need to present a valid ID.
- Passengers below 18 years oldtraveling from Davaomust presentTravel Permitissued by the City Social Welfare and Development Office (CSWDO)¬† or by the Special Office for Children's Concerns (SOCC) at check-in.
Forinternational travel, aDSWD travel clearanceis required if the minor is not traveling with a parent or legal guardian.
Yes. AChild Restraint System (CRS)that meetsFederal Motor Vehicle Safety Standards (FMVSS)or is certified by theCivil Aviation Authority (CAA)is required. Cebu Pacific does not provide CRS or car seats onboard, so these must be brought by the accompanying adult.
No. Cebu Pacific does not offer CRS or car seats. Passengers must bring their own if traveling with an infant who has a seat.
Each adult passenger may accompanyonly one (1) infant.
For group travel,one (1) adult is required for every 10 minors.

- This fee cannot be re-routed, refunded and cannot be stored in a Travel Fund.

üê£ The Infant Fee is charged to guests traveling with an infant because infants require special assistance.
- A guest is considered an infant if they areat least eight (8) days old to below two (2) years oldat the time of travel.
- The cost of this fee will be indicated in your booking summary.
With this, you¬†have the following options:
- Infant without seat- the infant will sit on the lap of the adult.
- Infant with seat- this infant (who must be at least 1 year old) can take the adjacent seat, charged at the lowest available fare.
- Please note that the arrangements cannot be changed once the booking has been paid.
üìñ To learn more about booking with infants and traveling with children in general, please visit these articles:
- Traveling with Minors and Infants
- Booking with Cebu Pacific
‚ùóPlease also be reminded of the following:
- Infants are NOT allowed to sit on the exit rows.
- If you decide to rebook a flight that involves an infant:The Infant Fee will be carried over to the new flight (as long as it remains unused).
- The Infant Fee will be carried over to the new flight (as long as it remains unused).

- International flights: from PHP 550 to PHP 950 per passenger.

### PH Travel Tax
‚òÄÔ∏èüå¥ In accordance with the¬†Tourism Infrastructure and Enterprise Zone Authority (TIEZA), the Philippine Travel Tax is a levy imposed by the Philippine government on individuals leaving the country. To learn more about this tax, you can check out theTIEZA page.üí° You'll need to pay for the PH Travel Tax if you're :
- A Philippine passport holder exiting the Philippines, or;
- A foreigner staying in the Philippines for more than a year.
- Foreign nationals staying less than a year are NOT required to pay for this tax.
- If you are an Overseas Filipino Worker (OFW):You arenot required to pay the travel taxif you are returning to the country where you are employed.However, if you are traveling as a tourist to a different country,¬†the travel taxstill applies.Your dependents may be eligible for thePrivileged Reduced Travel Taxwhen traveling to your country of employment.Learn more here:TIEZA - Reduced Travel Tax
- You arenot required to pay the travel taxif you are returning to the country where you are employed.
- However, if you are traveling as a tourist to a different country,¬†the travel taxstill applies.
- Your dependents may be eligible for thePrivileged Reduced Travel Taxwhen traveling to your country of employment.Learn more here:TIEZA - Reduced Travel Tax
- Learn more here:TIEZA - Reduced Travel Tax
- As per government regulations, the travel tax may only be refunded and cannot be stored in your Travel Fund.
- If you choose to rebook your flight, the travel tax will be carried over to your new booking.
‚úÖ The following guests are exempted from paying the PH Travel Tax:
Ov. Overseas Filipino Workers (OFW) returning to the country where they are employedüí°Take note!If you are an OFW traveling as a tourist to a different country, the travel taxstill applies.
Fi. Filipino permanent residents abroad whose stay in the Philippines is less than one year
In. Infants (2 years and below)
Fo. Foreign Diplomatic and Consular Officials and Members of their Staff
Of. Officials, Consultants, Experts, and Employees of the United Nations (UN) Organization and its agencies
Un. United States (US) Military Personnel including dependents and other US nationals with fares paid for by the US government or on US Government-owned or chartered transport facilities
Cr. Crewmembers of airplanes flying international routes
Ph. Philippine Foreign Service Personnel officially assigned abroad and their dependents (This does not apply to OFWs)
Of. Officials and Employees of the Philippine Government traveling on official business (excluding Government-Owned and Controlled Corporations)
Gr. Grantees of foreign government funded trips
Bo. Bona-fide Students with approved scholarships by appropriate government agency
Pe. Personnel (and their dependents) of multinational companies with regional headquarters, but not engaged in business, in the Philippines
Th. Those authorized by the President of the Republic of the Philippines for reasons of national interest
As. As provided under R.A. 6768, Balikbayans whose stay in the Philippines is less than one (1) year, and family members of former Filipinos accompanying the latter.
The PH Travel Tax can be easily paid for when you book a flight or manage your booking with Cebu Pacific. There is no need to approach the TIEZA counter if you've already paid for it.
To pay for the tax, simply follow the steps below:
- How to pay when booking
- How to pay after booking
‚úàÔ∏è Pay at the time of booking
Bo. Book a flight on the Cebu Pacific app.
Wh. While booking, you'll be asked to pay for the tax. Make sure to tick the box if you want to avoid long lines at the airport.
Af. After successful payment, the tax should now be reflected in the Fare Breakdown of the confirmation page.

### ‚úàÔ∏è If you forgot to pay at the time of booking
Lo. Log into your MyCebuPacific account and tap "My Bookings"
Sc. Scroll down until you see your booking and tap "Manage"üí°: Can't see your booking? You'll need toadd it to your accountfirst.
Sc. Scroll down and tap the "Philippine Travel Tax" box
Ti. Tick the box and proceed to pay for the PH Travel Tax
‚úàÔ∏è General Guidelines

- Please check here if you're exempted from paying:Travel Tax exemptions

Do. Download the eGovPH app on Google Play or the App Store
If. If you're using the app for the first time, sign up for an account using any valid government ID. Otherwise, simply log in.
Ta. Tap on NGAs
Sc. Scroll to the bottom of the page and tap on TIEZA
Pr. Proceed to tap on TIEZA Travel Tax
Fi. Fill out the passenger details. Check your Itinerary Receipt to ensure that you enter the correct details.üí° The details must match the information you will enter in your eTravel declaration form.
Pa. Pay for the tax and get your digital receipt. Once payment is successful, there is no need to approach¬†the TIEZA counter at the airport.

# How to Earn and Redeem Go Rewards Points
You can earn Go Rewards points every time you book a flight or buy add-ons online. You can then use those same points to pay for future flights!

## Overview

### Description
Earn Go Rewards points when you book a flight or buy the following add-ons:
- Seats
- Baggage
- Meals
- CEB Sports Equipment add-on
‚úàÔ∏è At the time of booking,¬†enter your Go Rewards number when filling out the Guest Details page:
- üí° To successfully earn points,make sure the name and email in your booking match the details in your Go Rewards account.Points are credited seven (7) days after you board your flight.To update the name in your Go Rewards membership account, please reach out to theGo Rewards Customer Care Team.Learn more here:How can I change my name on my Go Rewards account?
- Points are credited seven (7) days after you board your flight.
- To update the name in your Go Rewards membership account, please reach out to theGo Rewards Customer Care Team.
- Learn more here:How can I change my name on my Go Rewards account?
- If you forgot to add your Go Rewards number at the time of booking, you can easily add it later on via Manage Booking.Learn more here:Updating Your Guest or Contact DetailsYour Go Rewards number can no longer be added after the flight has been flown.
- Learn more here:Updating Your Guest or Contact Details
- Your Go Rewards number can no longer be added after the flight has been flown.
- Go Rewards points have no monetary value and are not convertible to cash.You may use your Go Rewards points to pay for your transactions with participating partners and merchants.For more information, visit¬†the Go RewardsTerms and Conditions.
- You may use your Go Rewards points to pay for your transactions with participating partners and merchants.
- For more information, visit¬†the Go RewardsTerms and Conditions.
- If your Go Rewards flight gets canceled or disrupted, it will be converted to a non-expiring Travel Fund.
- Lost your Go Rewards card or account number? Please contact theGo Rewards Customer Care Team.
For more information on earning and redeeming points, please visit theGo Rewards Help Center.

- Other Philippine government agencies that are allowed by law to secure the use of firearms and/or security items to enforce their functions.
Exemption will be subject to the following conditions:
- The exemption is valid for either one short or one long firearm (FA) at a time
- The exemption only applies to domestic travel
- The exemption is for the performance of official government functions

üê£ The Infant Fee is charged to guests traveling with an infant because infants require special assistance.
- A guest is considered an infant if they areat least eight (8) days old to below two (2) years oldat the time of travel.
- The cost of this fee will be indicated in your booking summary.
With this, you¬†have the following options:
- Infant without seat- the infant will sit on the lap of the adult.
- Infant with seat- this infant (who must be at least 1 year old) can take the adjacent seat, charged at the lowest available fare.
- Please note that the arrangements cannot be changed once the booking has been paid.

- International flights: from PHP 550 to PHP 950 per passenger.
- Domestic flights: from PHP 200 to PHP 390 per passenger.
- Whether you booked before or after the terminal fee increase:You do not need to pay any additional fees¬†at the airport.The updated fee has automatically been included in your total booking amount.

### PH Travel Tax
‚òÄÔ∏èüå¥ In accordance with the¬†Tourism Infrastructure and Enterprise Zone Authority (TIEZA), the Philippine Travel Tax is a levy imposed by the Philippine government on individuals leaving the country. To learn more about this tax, you can check out theTIEZA page.üí° You'll need to pay for the PH Travel Tax if you're :
- A Philippine passport holder exiting the Philippines, or;
- A foreigner staying in the Philippines for more than a year.
- Foreign nationals staying less than a year are NOT required to pay for this tax.
- If you are an Overseas Filipino Worker (OFW):You arenot required to pay the travel taxif you are returning to the country where you are employed.However, if you are traveling as a tourist to a different country,¬†the travel taxstill applies.Your dependents may be eligible for thePrivileged Reduced Travel Taxwhen traveling to your country of employment.Learn more here:TIEZA - Reduced Travel Tax
- You arenot required to pay the travel taxif you are returning to the country where you are employed.
- However, if you are traveling as a tourist to a different country,¬†the travel taxstill applies.
- Your dependents may be eligible for thePrivileged Reduced Travel Taxwhen traveling to your country of employment.Learn more here:TIEZA - Reduced Travel Tax
- Learn more here:TIEZA - Reduced Travel Tax
- As per government regulations, the travel tax may only be refunded and cannot be stored in your Travel Fund.
- If you choose to rebook your flight, the travel tax will be carried over to your new booking.
‚úÖ The following guests are exempted from paying the PH Travel Tax:
Ov. Overseas Filipino Workers (OFW) returning to the country where they are employedüí°Take note!If you are an OFW traveling as a tourist to a different country, the travel taxstill applies.
Fi. Filipino permanent residents abroad whose stay in the Philippines is less than one year
In. Infants (2 years and below)
Fo. Foreign Diplomatic and Consular Officials and Members of their Staff
Of. Officials, Consultants, Experts, and Employees of the United Nations (UN) Organization and its agencies
Un. United States (US) Military Personnel including dependents and other US nationals with fares paid for by the US government or on US Government-owned or chartered transport facilities
Cr. Crewmembers of airplanes flying international routes
Ph. Philippine Foreign Service Personnel officially assigned abroad and their dependents (This does not apply to OFWs)
Of. Officials and Employees of the Philippine Government traveling on official business (excluding Government-Owned and Controlled Corporations)
Gr. Grantees of foreign government funded trips
Bo. Bona-fide Students with approved scholarships by appropriate government agency
Pe. Personnel (and their dependents) of multinational companies with regional headquarters, but not engaged in business, in the Philippines
Th. Those authorized by the President of the Republic of the Philippines for reasons of national interest
As. As provided under R.A. 6768, Balikbayans whose stay in the Philippines is less than one (1) year, and family members of former Filipinos accompanying the latter.
The PH Travel Tax can be easily paid for when you book a flight or manage your booking with Cebu Pacific. There is no need to approach the TIEZA counter if you've already paid for it.
To pay for the tax, simply follow the steps below:
- How to pay when booking
- How to pay after booking

Wh. While booking, you'll be asked to pay for the tax. Make sure to tick the box if you want to avoid long lines at the airport.
Af. After successful payment, the tax should now be reflected in the Fare Breakdown of the confirmation page.

Your CEB Meal Add-on should carry over to your new flight if:
- You rebooked, and your new flight is more than 24 hours away.
If your new flight is less than 24h away:
- Disrupted flights: You will be refunded the value of your meal
- Voluntary rebooking: Your CEB Meals will be forfeited

- The voucher is assigned to a specific passenger name and cannot be transferred nor changed to another name.

- Additionally, unaccompanied minors who need POCs are not accepted onboard.

üíä If you need to bring other medical equipment (e.g. syringes, medicine, etc.)
- You may bring it free of charge. It will be exempt from your hand-carry limit.

# Updating Your Guest or Contact Details
Made a typo? You can go to Manage Booking within 24 hours of booking to change either your First or your Last Name! You can also update your other contact and guest details up to 2 hours before your flight.

## Overview

### Description

## ‚úèÔ∏èUpdate Name
- ‚ö†Ô∏è You can update either yourFirst Name only, or yourLast Name only;
- ‚è≥ You can only make this change within 24 hours from the time of booking completion;
- ‚òùÔ∏èYou can only update this once.
If it's more than 24 hours since you made your booking:
- üí¨ Pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can validate your request;
- üìÑ Please prepare proof of the name correction, e.g., marriage certificate, or other supporting documents.
Special characters in your name:
- If your name has special characters (e.g., √±, √©, √º) please replace them with the regular letter instead (e.g., Ni√±a ‚û°Ô∏è Nina).
- For names with apostrophes or hyphens, you may replace them with a space (e.g., Mary-Jane‚û°Ô∏è Mary Jane, O'Connor ‚û°Ô∏è O Connor).
- If your boarding pass or itinerary shows your name without special characters, don't worry! Your booking is still valid.
Suffixes in your name:
- If your name has a suffix (Jr., Sr., III), proceed to enter the suffix in the "First Name" field.
- Enter your name exactly as it is shown in your valid ID.
General Guidelines:
- üë§ An account is required to make any booking changes.
- ‚ùå Booking isNOTtransferable to another guest.

- ‚òùÔ∏è For nationality/passport, birthday, and salutation details, you can only update this once.
- ‚úåÔ∏è For your contact number, you can update this multiple times as necessary.
- Please approach the airport counters for assistance.
For OFWs, you can change or add your Overseas Employment Certificate (OEC) / MIAA Exemption Certificate (MEC) number even after completion of booking through the following channels:
- Chat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can validate your request.
- If you're at the airport, please approach theOverseas Workers Welfare Administration (OWWA) counter.
- Once you're at the counter, present any of these documents, OEC issued by the OWWA; OEC Balik Manggagawa Certificate; or MEC.

# CEB Seat Selector
Fly easy on your preferred seat! Choose a window seat for the view, an aisle seat for convenience, or a front row seat for extra legroom.

## Overview

### Description

## üí∫CEB Seat Selector
CEB Seat Selector lets you choose your preferred seat, so you can sit together, by the window, or near the exits!
You can purchase it when youbook a flight, or through Manage Booking on theCebu Pacific app.
| Seat class
| Benefits
| ‚ú® Premium
| Extra legroomSeat near exit & lavatoryPriority boarding (except for Macau, China, and Dubai)
- Extra legroom
- Seat near exit & lavatory
- Priority boarding (except for Macau, China, and Dubai)
| ‚ûï Standard Plus:
| Extra legroomSeat near exit & lavatory
| üü° Standard:
| Seat of your choice
If you didn't buy Seat Selector, don't worry:
- ‚úÖ Everyone with a ticket is guaranteed a seat on the aircraft.
- üé≤ You will be assigned a random seat at check-inIf you're traveling with multiple guests, there's a chance you won't be seated together.If you're traveling with children, we recommend buying your seats in advance üòä
- If you're traveling with multiple guests, there's a chance you won't be seated together.
- If you're traveling with children, we recommend buying your seats in advance üòä
- Requesting for Medical, Mobility, and Travel Assistance
General Guidelines:
- üë§ A MyCebuPacific account is required to buy, add or change a seat.Sign upnow!
- ‚åõ Seat Selector is available via Manage Booking up to 2 hours before your flight.

## Policies & Guides

### Airline Policies
Passengers who want to sit in an exit row seat must be able to fulfill safety requirements and meet the criteria below:
- Be at least 15 years old.
- Be able to speak and understand English to follow instructions given onboard.
- Be physically fit and able to reach, open, lift, and throw out the exit door in an emergency.
- Not be pregnant or seated with an infant or a passenger under 15 years old.
- Not have any permanent or temporary impairments (e.g., hearing or vision impairments, strength or mobility limitations, cognitive differences, or traveling with a service or emotional support animal).
These guidelines align with international safety standards to ensure the well-being of everyone on board. Our Cabin Crew may reseat passengers who do not meet these criteria.
GO Ahead Priority Boarding is a feature of the Premium category of CEB Seat Selector.¬†Please note that boarding procedures vary per airport, and some may require transport using a bus or shuttle from the gate to the aircraft.

## ‚úã Voluntary cancelation
Please be reminded that pre-purchased add-ons arenon-cancelableandnon-refundable.
For more information, visit this article:Rebooking or Canceling Your Flight

## üí° Carrying over / rebooking of CEB Seat Selector Add-on
- You rebooked your flight;
- Your flight was changed by more than 1 hour;
- Your flight was cancelled, and you moved to a different flight.

Pr. Proceed to pay for your flight
Lo. Log into your MyCebuPacific account and tap "My Bookings"
Sc. Scroll down until you see your booking and tap "Manage"üí°: Can't see your booking? You'll need toadd it to your accountfirst.
Un. Under Modify flight, tap "Manage add-ons"
On. Once you reach the add-ons page, tap on "CEB Seat Selector"
Pr. Proceed to pay
If your child is in need of a bassinet, look out for the bassinet icon while selecting seats.

- You may bring it free of charge. It will be exempt from your hand-carry limit.
