# Traveling with Service and Emotional Support Animals
Cebu Pacific welcomes dogs onboard as either service animals or emotional support animals. No other animals are allowed in the cabin.

## Overview

### Description

## üê∂ What's the difference?
| Type
| Service Dog
| Trained to perform specific tasks for individuals with reduced mobilities (i.e., seeing eye / hearing dog).
| Emotional Support Dog
| Provides comfort and emotional stability to help ease anxiety and depression through companionship. Not task-trained.
General Guidelines:
- Make sure to declare that you'll be bringing your dog with you at the time of booking or via Manage Booking.
- Only one (1) dog is allowed per flight.

## ‚úàÔ∏èAccepted Flights
| Flight
| Service Dogs
| Emotional Support Dogs
| Cebu Pacific (5J)
| ‚úÖ accepted
| Cebgo (DG)
| AirSWIFT (T6)
| ‚ùå not yet accepted; coming soon!
Other household pets may be shipped viaCEB Cargoonly.

## üìã Travel Requirements
| 1.Document confirming the service dog has been trained
| 1.Document with letterhead from your medical doctor supporting the need for emotional support animal
| 2.Complete and up-to-date vaccination card of the dog
| 3. Shipping permit issued by the Bureau of Animal Industry - Department of Agriculture
| 3.Shipping permit issued by the Bureau of Animal Industry - Department of Agriculture

## üêæ Accessories &¬†Setup
- Service Dogs:Must be securelyleashedat all times; not required to wear a mouth-restraint device (i.e., muzzle, mouthguard, mouth cover, collar).
- Emotional Support Dogs:Allowed inside asoft carrierthat fits under the seat (approx. 8in x 8in x 14in).If inside a soft carrier, a leash and mouth-restraint device are not required.If outside a soft carrier, both a leash and a mouth‚Äërestraint device are required.
- If inside a soft carrier, a leash and mouth-restraint device are not required.
- If outside a soft carrier, both a leash and a mouth‚Äërestraint device are required.

## üí∫ Seating Guidelines
- Dogscannot occupy a seator be seated in theexit row.
- Must fit on your lap or within your legroom.
Recommended setup:
- Sit by the window with your dog between you and the window.
If your dog is too large:
- You may be moved to a seat with extra space (if available).
- If the flight is full, you may be rebooked to a later flight to accommodate you and your dog better.
- To guarantee space,purchase an extra seat.Chat with usso we can help you purchase an extra seat.

## üßº Hygiene & Comfort
- Service and emotional support dogs must wearpet diapersand sit onmoisture-absorbing material.
- Alternatively, provide a document stating your dogdoes not need to relieve itselfduring the flight.

## üåé Government Clearances
- All animals imported, transhipped, or exported to/fromSingaporerequire a validAnimal & Veterinary Service (AVS)license.
- For travel to/fromAustralia,refer to this articlefor Seeing Eye dog guidelines.

## FAQs

### General FAQs

PWD/senior citizen discounts
Please take note of the following:
- Filipino nationals who are senior citizens and/or PWDs are entitled to a 20% discount and VAT exemption on domestic flights.
- The discount does not apply to promo fares or seat sale flights,and can only be applied when you first book.
- The senior citizen discount will automatically apply once you enter your birthday in the Guest Details page.
- The senior/PWD discount cannot be applied to flights that have already been booked.
You are¬†required to present the following identification at the airport:
- Senior Citizens:
- Senior Citizen ID issued by the Office for Senior Citizen Affairs (OSCA) orAny government-issued ID with your name, picture, date of birth, and nationality.
- Senior Citizen ID issued by the Office for Senior Citizen Affairs (OSCA) or
- Any government-issued ID with your name, picture, date of birth, and nationality.
- PWDs:A valid ID issued by a local government unit orA valid ID from the National Council on Disability Affairs (NCDA).
- A valid ID issued by a local government unit or
- A valid ID from the National Council on Disability Affairs (NCDA).

| Fare Bundle
| Inclusions
| GO Basic
| Voluntary cancellation:Not allowed, available withCEB Flexi add-on.Baggage allowance:7kg hand-carry only.Seat Selector:Random seat assigned at check-in.Voluntary rebooking:Allowed but subject to change fees and fare differences.Name correction:First Name or Last Name only. General Guidelines:

- The bundle will apply to all guests in the booking.

- You cannot switch your bundle to another (e.g. from GO Basic to GO Easy).
- üíº You can add or upgrade your baggage allowance after you select a fare bundle.

AnInfant Feewill be applied to guests traveling with an infant due to the special assistance required. Guests have the following options:
- Infant without seat:The infant will sit on the adult's lap.No baggage allowance will be given for infants on lap.
- The infant will sit on the adult's lap.

- Infant with seat:The infant will occupy their own seat next to the parent/guardian's‚Äîcharged at the lowest available fare.The infant will have their own hand-carry baggage allowance. - Infants with seat are required to have a Child Restraint System (CRS) that conforms to Federal Motor Vehicle Safety Standards (FMVSS) or certified by the Civil Aviation Authority (CAA).
- For their safety, infants below 8 days old will not be accepted for carriage.
- Infants can only travel if accompanied by an adult aged 18 years and above. Only one (1) infant is allowed per adult passenger.

- Make sure you set them as "Children" when you first book your flight.

- Traveling internationally alone, or

# How to Manage Your Disrupted Flight
Manage disrupted flights anywhere ‚Äî no need to visit the airport!

## Overview

### Description

## General Guidelines
While we continuously work to ensure your flight departs and arrives on time, on-the-spot delays or cancelations may occur due to environmental, operational or technical reasons.
- Affected passengers will be notified by Cebu Pacific frontline team, email, and/or text message.
- You can check the real-time status of your flight through ourFlight Status page.
- We will ensure your welfare is taken care of whenever there are planned or on-the-spot changes to flights.Know your rights as an air passenger through this article:Passenger Rights & Airline PoliciesCheck the applicable options for on-the-spot disruptions:Disruptions at the airport
- Know your rights as an air passenger through this article:Passenger Rights & Airline Policies
- Passenger Rights & Airline Policies
- Check the applicable options for on-the-spot disruptions:Disruptions at the airport
- Disruptions at the airport
After being notified of the disruption, you will be given a link to our Self-Service Disruption Portal (SSDP).
You may also access this by going toManage Bookingon the Cebu Pacific app or website.

## üìù Disruption options
We offer the following flexible options for disrupted guests:
- Rebook your flightRebook your flight for free up to 30 days before or 30 days after your original schedule.If you need to rebook beyond the 30-day period,pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help.
Rebook your flight

- Request a refundRequest a refund of your fare according to your form of payment.Travel Tax and unused TravelSure will have to be refunded separately.Learn more here:Refund Concerns
Request a refund
- Request a refund of your fare according to your form of payment.
- Travel Tax and unused TravelSure will have to be refunded separately.
- Learn more here:Refund Concerns
- Convert to Travel FundWhen converting your disrupted flight to Travel Fund, it¬†will be stored in yourbooking reference number.With this, you can use it to pay for future flights or add-ons.Once you reach the payment page, simply enter thesix-digit booking reference numberthat contains the Travel Fund.Learn more about the Travel Fund here:CEB Flexi & Travel Fund
Convert to Travel Fund
- When converting your disrupted flight to Travel Fund, it¬†will be stored in yourbooking reference number.
- With this, you can use it to pay for future flights or add-ons.
- Once you reach the payment page, simply enter thesix-digit booking reference numberthat contains the Travel Fund.
- Learn more about the Travel Fund here:CEB Flexi & Travel Fund
- üí°Remember!Once you pick an option, it's final and can't be changed or undone.You can only rebook, refund, or convert your disrupted flight to Travel Fundonce.When rebooking, make sure you're selecting the correct flight dates!
- Once you pick an option, it's final and can't be changed or undone.

# Passenger Rights and Airline Policies
Is your flight disrupted? Know your rights as an air passenger!

## Overview

### Description
- Cebu Pacific aims to keep passengers informed, especially when there are flight changes, so you can make alternative plans.
- If schedule changes or disruptions happen, notifications may be provided through email, text message, Cebu Pacific's social networking sites, Cebu Pacific website, airport screens, and/or airport or onboard announcements.

## üìú Provision of Options
- To ensure passenger's welfare is taken care of whenever there are flight changes, Cebu Pacific will provide options based on the Philippine Air Passenger Bill of Rights.

# CEB Baggage Guidelines and Upgrade Options
Bringing home extra pasalubong, or planning out your OOTDs?   If you need to bring more things, you can add CEB Baggage and CEB Special Baggage to your booking. It's available through Manage Booking up to 2 hours before your flight!

## üß≥Checked baggage allowance
Checked baggage allowance is only included in our GO Easy and GO Flexi fare bundles:
| Fare Bundle
| Checked baggage allowance
| GO Basic
| ‚ùå None(Available as Add-on)
| GO Easy
| ‚úÖ 1 piece, 20kg allowance(Size limit: 39x39x39in)
| GO Flexi
For every 20kg of prepaid baggage allowance, you are entitled to bring one (1) piece of checked baggage.

## ‚ûïBaggage Upgrade and Extra Piece Purchase
- If you need toincrease the weight of your 20kg checked baggage, you may upgrade by 4kg, 8kg, or up to 12kg.Please note that upgrading the weight does not change the number of pieces allowed.
- Please note that upgrading the weight does not change the number of pieces allowed.
- If you need toincrease the number of pieces of your checked baggage, you can purchase a maximum of three (3) pieces online, with each piece having a base weight of 20kg.Should you require more than three pieces, additional baggage can be purchased at the airport.This does not apply to flights departingBangkok (BKK)andDon Mueang (DMK), where a temporary baggage policy limits airport purchases to two (2) pieces only.
- Should you require more than three pieces, additional baggage can be purchased at the airport.This does not apply to flights departingBangkok (BKK)andDon Mueang (DMK), where a temporary baggage policy limits airport purchases to two (2) pieces only.
- This does not apply to flights departingBangkok (BKK)andDon Mueang (DMK), where a temporary baggage policy limits airport purchases to two (2) pieces only.
- üí° If you need to bring larger or specialized items, consider gettingCEB Special Baggage Add-on.

## üëú Hand-carry allowance
| Hand-carry allowance
| ‚úÖ 1 piece for overhead binand 1 piece for under the seat, 7kg allowance(Size limit: 22inx 14in x 10in for baggage in the overhead bin and8in x 8in x 14in for baggage under the seat)

------------------------------------------------------------
# Airport Baggage Guidelines
If you weren't able to buy baggage allowance ahead of time, or exceed the maximum weights or dimensions, you may be charged additional fees at the airport.

## Overview

### Description
To avoid high airport baggage fees,pre-purchase your CEB baggage allowance online. Learn more:CEB Baggage Guidelines and Upgrade Options
üí°You‚Äôll be charged an airport baggage fee if:
- You didn‚Äôt buy your checked baggage allowance online.
- You exceed the number of allowed baggage pieces.
- Your bag exceeds size or weight limits.
‚ö†Ô∏èExcess Baggage Fee
- Chargedper kiloover your allowance.
- Example: If you bought 20kg but check in 23kg, you‚Äôll pay for 3kg extra.
- No single bag can exceed 32kg.
üëúGate Baggage Fee
- Charged if yourhand-carry exceeds the allowed limit of 7kgs.
- Fees vary by booking date and regulations.
‚úÖAvoid extra fees by:
- Buying the right baggage allowance in advance.
- Keeping bags within size and weight limits.

# CEB Special Baggage
Got oversized items for your trip? We accept special baggage like sports equipment, surfboards, musical instruments, and oversized bags for check-in, for a fee. Learn more below.

## Overview

### Description
- CEB Special Baggage is available up to two (2) hours before your flight.To add CEB Special Baggage to your booking, manage your booking via theCebu Pacific app.A MyCebuPacific account is required to buy or add CEB Special Baggage.Sign upnow!
- To add CEB Special Baggage to your booking, manage your booking via theCebu Pacific app.A MyCebuPacific account is required to buy or add CEB Special Baggage.Sign upnow!
- A MyCebuPacific account is required to buy or add CEB Special Baggage.Sign upnow!
- Each guest is only allowed one (1) of each kind of special baggage, and with a weight of 20kg each.
- However, if a guest brings more than 20kg, they will need to pay an¬†excess baggage fee.Take note! Baggage can be increased to a maximum weight of 32kg.
- Take note! Baggage can be increased to a maximum weight of 32kg.
- CEB Special Baggage may not be available on Cebgo (DG) flights due to limited space.
üí°For instructions on adding regular baggage allowance to your booking, please visit theCEB Baggage Guidelines and Upgrade Optionsarticle.

------------------------------------------------------------
# Lost, Damaged, or Delayed Baggage
What to do and where to reach out to if your baggage gets damaged, missing, or lost

## Overview

### Description

## üß≥ General Guidelines
The policies below apply tochecked baggageonly.
- If you lost/left items in the aircraft:Immediately report it to any Cebu Pacific ground staff,orchat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help.
- Immediately report it to any Cebu Pacific ground staff,
- orchat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help.
- If you lost items at the¬†airport,Contact the airport‚ÄôsLost & Found officedirectly.
- Contact the airport‚ÄôsLost & Found officedirectly.
If your checked baggage was damaged, or did not arrive at your destination airport:
- Do not leave the airport;
- Immediately report it to any Cebu Pacific ground staff;
- Our staff will assist you in filing a Property Irregularity Report (PIR).

## ü©π Damaged Baggage
If yourchecked baggagearrived with a cracked surface or missing handle and/or wheels:
- We will assess if the damage exceeds¬†regular wear and tear;
- If so, we will provide compensation based on Philippine Air Passenger Bill of Rights or the Montreal Convention.

## üõÖ Missing / Delayed Baggage
If yourchecked baggagedid not arrive with you at the destination airport, please report it immediately.
While we locate your baggage, we will also provide you with the following delay compensation:
- üíµ Php2,000 for every 24 hours of delay
- üí≥If checked baggage is not delivered within 24 hours, the applicable baggage fees will be refunded.
We will notify you of the total compensation within 7 days of reporting.

## üîç Lost Baggage
If yourchecked baggageisn't found within 7 days of your arrival, we will consider your baggage lost.
We will compensate you with the value of the lost baggage, along with the delay compensation mentioned above.

## FAQ

### Other Policies
üß≥ Damaged or Missing Baggage?
If your checked baggage is damaged or missing,immediately report it to any Cebu Pacific staff while still at the airport. Our team will assist you in filing aProperty Irregularity Report (PIR).
üìåImportant:PIRs can only be filedwithin the airport premisesfor proper validation. Once you leave the airport, we can no longer accommodate PIR filing.
‚úÖSave your PIR Numberfor reference.
üì© We‚Äôll keep you updated on your baggage status via the email and/or mobile number you provided.
‚è≥ If you don‚Äôt receive an update within 24 hours, please reach out to us via chat on our app or website.
- Pick up the baggage from the destination airport; or
- Arrange for delivery to your registered address.
If your baggage is mistakenly claimed by another passenger and has been recovered, you need to pick up the recovered baggage at the airport.
If you mistakenly claimed someone else's baggage, please go back to the airport and inform any of the Cebu Pacific ground staff.

# Redeeming Your Travel Voucher
Know more about how to book Cebu Pacific flights using your issued Travel Voucher.

## Overview

### Description

## üé´ Travel Vouchers
Travel Vouchers are free tickets issued by Cebu Pacific in certain situations.It covers thebase fareof any future travel plans you may have!These vouchers are non-transferrable, non-rebookable, and doesn't cover fees or other taxes.
‚úàÔ∏èGeneral Guidelines:
- The Travel Voucher is sent to you via email.Please check the email you used to book the flight for the latest updates.You may also check if you have a travel voucher by logging in to your MyCebuPacific account.
- Please check the email you used to book the flight for the latest updates.
- You may also check if you have a travel voucher by logging in to your MyCebuPacific account.
- The voucher is assigned to a specific passenger name and cannot be transferred nor changed to another name.
- The voucher is also assigned to a specific flight type and cannot be changed to another origin/destination.
- The voucher cannot be converted to Travel Fund or in the form of a refund.
- These vouchers usually include the following flight types:Domestic One-wayDomestic Round-tripInternational One-way (Short haul)International Round-trip (Short haul)International One-Way (Long haul)International Round-trip (Long haul)
- Domestic One-way
- Domestic Round-trip
- International One-way (Short haul)
- International Round-trip (Short haul)
- International One-Way (Long haul)
- International Round-trip (Long haul)
- Know more about where we fly in this article:Cebu Pacific Destinations, Airports, and Terminal Numbers
- If you're experiencing issues with your Travel Voucher, check out ourtroubleshooting steps.
üå¥Travel Vouchers are not allowed for use during peak travel periods.Please take note of the peak travel periods below:

[130] What to Expect During Tarmac Delays
URL      : https://help.cebupacificair.com/article/what-to-expect-during-tarmac-delays-97601
CATEGORY : Cancelations & Delays
------------------------------------------------------------
# What to Expect During Tarmac Delays

## Overview

### Description
EffectiveMarch 15, 2024,Cebu Pacific follows thiscontingency planto ensure your comfort and safety during long tarmac delays. This is in line with the Joint Memorandum Circular No. 001 issued by the Department of Transportation (DOT), Civil Aeronautics Board (CAB), Civil Aviation Authority of the Philippines (CAAP), and Manila International Airport Authority (MIAA).
What Is a Tarmac Delay?A tarmac delay happens when:
- Your plane is waiting on the runway or taxiway for two (2) hours or more, either before takeoff or after landing; and
- You are not allowed to get off the plane due to safety, security, or air traffic control reasons.
What the Pilot Will Do During a DelayThe Pilot-in-Command (PIC) is responsible for keeping you informed and comfortable. During a tarmac delay:
- You‚Äôll receive updates every 30 minutes about the reason for the delay and any changes; and
- The cabin crew will do their best to make sure you're comfortable while waiting.
Getting Off the Plane (Deplaning)If the tarmac delay reaches three (3) hours, the pilot will begin letting passengers off the plane unless:
- It's unsafe or not allowed by airport authorities;
- Air traffic control says moving the plane would disrupt airport operations;
- The flight is expected to take off within 30 minutes after the three (3) hour mark;
- There's no clean and safe area at the airport to accommodate passengers who get off.
- If needed, Cebu Pacific may decide to return to the departure airport or land at a different airport to let passengers off safely.
Food and DrinksOnce the tarmac delay reaches two (2) hours, the cabin crew will start handing out food and water. If supplies are limited, priority will be given to:
- Passengers with special needs
- Passengers with small children
- Senior citizens and pregnant women
- If more food is needed, the cabin crew will request additional supplies from Cebu Pacific. For international flights, any unused pre-ordered meals may also be distributed.
Onboard ComfortWhile you're waiting on the plane, Cebu Pacific will make sure that:
- Toilets are working;
- Air conditioning is functioning; and
- Medical help is available if needed
At the Airport After Getting OffIf passengers are allowed to get off the plane:
- Cebu Pacific's team will work with the airport staff to make sure there's a clean and safe waiting area.
- Special attention will be given to:Passengers with special needs;Parents with small children;Senior citizens and pregnant women;Unaccompanied minors; andPassengers with connecting flights.
- Passengers with special needs;
- Parents with small children;
- Senior citizens and pregnant women;
- Unaccompanied minors; and
- Passengers with connecting flights.
- Food, water, and communication services will be provided to passengers.
- Updates will also continue every 30 minutes until the flight resumes.
Need to Call Someone?If you've gotten off the plane, you can use the airport station's official phone to contact family or make arrangements for your next flight.
Reporting to AuthoritiesCebu Pacific will submit a report to the Civil Aeronautics Board (CAB) and Civil Aviation Authority of the Philippines (CAAP) within three (3) days of any long tarmac delay. This report will explain why passengers couldn't get off the plane and include supporting documents.
Did you find this article helpful?

# Signing up for a MyCebuPacific Account
With a Cebu Pacific account, you can easily manage your bookings and add-ons, receive promo alerts, and keep track of your Travel Fund! Read on to learn more.

## Overview

### Description

## üë§ MyCebuPacific Account
Create a Cebu Pacific account to manage your bookings and add-ons, get promo alerts, manage your Travel Fund, and more!
Here are the benefits when you sign up for a MyCebuPacific account:
- Get updated on seat sales and promos!
- Easily manage your bookingsConveniently rebook a flight or purchase add-ons for a more comfortable flight
- Conveniently rebook a flight or purchase add-ons for a more comfortable flight
- Redeem your Travel Vouchers and Travel Fund
- Secure your bookings with¬†multi-factor authentication
Signing up is free and easy!

- Your nameIf you don't have a first name,simply tick the "I have no first name" box and fill in the remaining fields.

- üí°Tip:This should be the same email address used in your previous bookings. It makes adding existing Travel Fund (if any) much easier!
- You can also use your Google, Facebook or Apple accounts to quickly sign in.
General Guidelines:
- üë§ An account is required to manage or make changes to your booking.
- Anyone aged 18 and above is eligible for a MyCebuPacific account.
- Travel agencies, corporations, and government agencies are not eligible to sign up.
- When a booking is added or linked to your account, other guests cannot modify the booking.
- Your MyCebuPacific account is secured and protected via multi-factor authentication.Cebu Pacific uses the latest technology and meets regulatory standards in protecting customer data and transactions.
- Cebu Pacific uses the latest technology and meets regulatory standards in protecting customer data and transactions.

[136] CEB Flexi and Travel Fund
URL      : https://help.cebupacificair.com/article/ceb-flexi-and-travel-fund-123947
CATEGORY : Check-in & Boarding
------------------------------------------------------------
# CEB Flexi and Travel Fund
Book your flight with CEB Flexi for more savings and flexibility in your travel plans. Cancel your flight for FREE and convert the value of your booking to a Travel Fund!

## Overview

### Description

## üìÜ CEB Flexi
Change of plans? No problem. With CEB Flexi, you can cancel your trip for free.
It allows you to cancel your booking and convert its value to a non-expiring Travel Fund.
- Cancelation is available up to two (2) hours before departure
- You can then use this Travel Fund to pay for your future travel plans!
Once you convert to Travel Fund, it will appear in your account within 24 hours.
General Guidelines:
- CEB Flexi only allows for free cancellation;It does not cover rebooking change fees.
- It does not cover rebooking change fees.
- You cannot add CEB Flexi after you've finished booking your flight;
- The price of CEB Flexi is based on your flight date, and on regulatory guidelines.
- If you purchased CEB Flexi without a MyCebuPacific account, and you intend to cancel your flight later on:Pleasesign up or log into your MyCebuPacific account first.Remember!An account is required to make booking changes.Check out ourhow-to guidesto know how to voluntarily cancel your flight and convert it to Travel Fund with CEB Flexi.
- Pleasesign up or log into your MyCebuPacific account first.
- Remember!An account is required to make booking changes.
- Check out ourhow-to guidesto know how to voluntarily cancel your flight and convert it to Travel Fund with CEB Flexi.

## ü™ô Travel Fund
Travel Fund is a non-expiring virtual wallet that you can use to pay for your future trips. It's available if:
- You purchased CEB Flexi and used it to cancel your flight, or;
- Your flight was disrupted (i.e. canceled or had a 1hr+ schedule change).How to Manage Your Disrupted Flight
- How to Manage Your Disrupted Flight
- Guest/s in the booking has a serious illness, or has died;Guest's immediate family member has died.
- Guest's immediate family member has died.
- AMyCebuPacific Accountis required to make booking changes;
- Once you convert to Travel Fund, it will appear in your MyCebuPacific account within 24 hours;
- The currency of your Travel Fund will depend on what currency you used when booking your flight.
- The Travel Fund can be split among guests in the same booking.With this, pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help you.
- With this, pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help you.
- ‚ùå The Travel Fund cannot be exchanged or converted to cash.
When you convert a booking to Travel Fund, it includes:
- Fares and taxes;
- All unused add-ons
- Admin and handling fees.
Conversion to Travel Fund does not include:
- Travel taxas this is refunded separately;
- Cost of CEB Flexi;
- Cost ofCEB TravelSure insuranceas this is refunded separately;
- Flight fees, such as the hold fee and cancel fee (if applicable).

# Unaccompanied Minor Requirements
Unaccompanied Minors are guests aged 7 to below 12 years old at the time of travel. Learn more about the requirements and crucial reminders for minors traveling alone.

## Overview

### Description
- 7 to 11 years old at the time of travel;
- Traveling alone without an adult companion who is at least 18 years old; and
- Traveling within the Philippines.
- Children below 7 years old:They won't be allowed to board without an adult companion who is at least 18 years old.
- Minors aged 12 and above: They are considered adult guests, and do not require the UM Service.
- Minors on international flights: They won't be allowed to board without an adult companion who is¬†at least 18 years old.
This service is provided to ensure the child‚Äôs safety and comfort during the flight. The cost of Unaccompanied Minor Fee is indicated when you book your flight.

## üìù General Guidelines
To avail of the UM Service, the parent/guardian must:
- Complete the Passenger Handling Form.Please fill this out at least 24 hours before your flight.
- Please fill this out at least 24 hours before your flight.
- Pay for the Unaccompanied Minor Fee;
- Endorse the child at the check-in counter.Please present their valid ID, along with the child's travel documents;
- Please present their valid ID, along with the child's travel documents;
- Stay at the airport until the child's flight has departed.
Important Reminders:
- The UM Service is only available on domestic flights.
- The UM Service is not available for minors who need Portable Oxygen Concentrators (POC)For their safety, they must travel with an adult companion who is at least 18 years old.
- For their safety, they must travel with an adult companion who is at least 18 years old.
- We can only accept a limited number of unaccompanied minors per flight.Make sure you set them as "Children" when you first book your flight.
- Make sure you set them as "Children" when you first book your flight.
üìùFilipino minors (under 18) need a travel clearancefrom the Department of Social Welfare and Development (DSWD) if they are:
- Traveling internationally alone, or
- Traveling internationally with someone other than their parents or legal guardian.
This permit states that it is with full knowledge of the parents that the child is travelling out of the country.
- To apply for travel clearance, use DSWD‚ÄôsMinors Traveling Abroad System. Walk-in applications will not be entertained.
- For online application guidance, watch thisvideo.
For minors with foreign nationalities,please check the rules governing minor travel as issued by your respective governments.

## ‚úàÔ∏è Traveling to and from Davao City
- They are traveling alone, or
- Traveling with a person other than their parents/legal guardians.
Below are the required documents for the permit to travel:
Bi. Birth Certificate of the minor (original and photocopy)
Ba. Barangay Clearance issued by the Punong Barangay, stating that the barangay has knowledge of the travel plans of the minor
Wr. Written parental consent attested by the Punong Barangay (if no parents, consent shall be made by the grandparents or eldest¬†sibling)
Id. Identification Card of the minor (original and photocopy)
Id. Identification Card of the authorized person who will accompany the child in his travels (original and photocopy).
If a child/minor is traveling with both or any of their parents,there is no need to secure a permitas long as there is a document to¬†prove the minor's relations such as:
Bi. Birth Certificate
Va. Valid IDs

## üìù Other Info
- If you need to rebook an unaccompanied minor's flight, you won't have to pay for the UM fee again.
- If you made a separate booking for a Child guest, but you will be traveling on the same flight as them:Chat with us via app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can refund the UM Fee.
- Chat with us via app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can refund the UM Fee.

# Online Travel Agency (OTA) Bookings
Learn more about bookings created with third-party channels.

## FAQ

### Online travel agencies
Authorized agencies
- Authorized Online Travel Agencies (OTAs) are online travel agents affiliated with Cebu Pacific who have secured the rightful permissions to display our flights on their website.
- Booking with authorized agencies ensures that you can seamlessly check in online and manage your booking on the Cebu Pacific app or website.Learn more here:Managing your travel agency booking
- Learn more here:Managing your travel agency booking
Unauthorized agencies
Booking with unauthorized online travel agencies may pose several issues, such as:
- Limited customer support: In case of flight disruptions or refunds, it may be difficult to reach out to the agency's customer service.
- No direct communication: Booking with unauthorized agencies can limit your ability to communicate directly with us, which is crucial for managing your bookings, requests, or emergencies.
- Security risk:Such agencies may not have secure payment processes, increasing the risk of your personal information being compromised.
- Unreliable bookings: There is a higher chance of errors, such as not being able to receive your itinerary and our system not recognizing your booking reference number.
‚úÖ Book directly with Cebu Pacific
Make sure to book with us via our website(https://www.cebupacificair.com/)or mobile app.

- Receive real-time updates for your flight.Get important notifications, such as flight updates, directly from us.

- Booking directly with us ensures your payment and personal details are handled securely.

- Book flights, check in, get your boarding pass, and upgrade baggage all in one app.
- Look out for theVerified by CEBbadge to ensure that you're booking with us directly.

Please take note that Cebu Pacific issues six-digit booking reference numbers.
‚úàÔ∏è General Guidelines
- To request for a refund, you may either do the following:Reach out to the online travel agency in order for them to process a refund for your booking, orFill out theGuest Feedback Form, orChat with usto connect with a live agent who can help you.
- Reach out to the online travel agency in order for them to process a refund for your booking, or
- Fill out theGuest Feedback Form, or
- Refunds are usually processed by Cebu Pacific within 15 days and is subject to our fare rules.
- Depending on the payment method used for the booking, it may take up to 2 billing cycles for your refund to be credited.
‚úÖ You may request for a refund under the following circumstances:
- Your flight was cancelled by us
- You are a pregnant mother unfit to fly
- You, or another passenger in the booking has a serious illness, or has diedor an immediate family member of yours or another passenger has recently died

- Medical, mobility and travel assistance

- Unaccompanied Minor (UM) service

If your flight gets disrupted (e.g. delayed, changes to flight time), it's possible that you won't receive notifications about it.
- This is because the email that was used to book the flight may not belong to you, so you may not be getting updates directly.
- For cases like this, we recommend contacting the online travel agency you booked with.

## ü©∫ Medical assistance
üöë Guests who are recovering from a major illness or surgery are welcome on board.
- Pleasedeclare your requestno later than four (4) hours before your flight.
- Request a medical certificate from your doctor indicating that you are "Fit to Travel".
ü´Å If you need to bring a Personal Oxygen Concentrator (POC):
- You may bring it free of charge. Please declare it no later than two (2) hours before your flight.
- We only accept FAA-approved POCs that can fit in the overhead bin, or under the aircraft seat.
- Air transport of partially or fully filled oxygen tanks (cylinders/bottles) or liquid oxygen is not allowed.Additionally, unaccompanied minors who need POCs are not accepted onboard.
- Additionally, unaccompanied minors who need POCs are not accepted onboard.
- Request a medical certificate from your doctor indicating the need to use the POC in-flight.
- Please present the POC and other respiratory assistive device and paperwork to a Cebu Pacific check-in agent.
üíä If you need to bring other medical equipment (e.g. syringes, medicine, etc.)
- You may bring it free of charge. It will be exempt from your hand-carry limit.

If you aremore than 34 weeks pregnant:
If you, or another guest has a severe Psychosocial Disability:
- They must be accompanied by at least 2 adult companions.
- If you need assistance at the airport, please declare your request no later than two (2) hours before your flight.

## üí∫Prisoners on board
- It is mandatory that for every prisoner, at least one (1) security officer from the PNP or NBI is present.
- The special handling must be arranged with Cebu Pacific at least 24 hours before the flight.

## Policies & Guides

### How to declare or request assistance
Bo. Book a flight on the Cebu Pacific app
On. Once you reach the Guest Details page, scroll down and tick the "I have a declaration / request" boxüí° You can make another declaration by tapping "Add another".
Lo. Log into your MyCebuPacific account on the mobile app and tap "My Bookings"
Sc. Scroll down until you see your booking and tap "Manage"üí°: Can't see your booking? You'll need toadd it to your accountfirst.
Ta. Tap on "Update Guest Details" underModify Flight
Sc. Scroll down and tick the "I have a declaration / request" box.üí° Is the declaration box greyed out?- This may be happening because you've already checked in or your flight is less than 4 hours away.- Please request for assistance at the airport counters instead.
Ta. Tap the "Update guest details" button once you're done

### Other policies
Filipino Nationals who are Senior Citizens and or PWDs are entitled to a 20% discount and VAT exemption on domestic flights.
The discount does not apply to promo fares or seat sale flights, and can only be applied when you first book.
You are¬†required to present the following identification at the airport:
- Senior Citizens:Senior Citizen ID issued by the Office for Senior Citizen Affairs (OSCA) or;Any government-issued ID with your name, picture, date of birth, and nationality.
- Senior Citizen ID issued by the Office for Senior Citizen Affairs (OSCA) or;
- Any government-issued ID with your name, picture, date of birth, and nationality.
- PWDs:A valid ID issued by a local government unit or;A valid ID from the National Council on Disability Affairs (NCDA).
- A valid ID issued by a local government unit or;
- A valid ID from the National Council on Disability Affairs (NCDA).
We have designated window seats for PWDs and PRMs, to prevent you from being disturbed by other passengers during boarding.
You will be given priority boarding and will be the last to deplane. If you would like to choose your seat, you may purchaseCEB Seat Selector Ad-on.
- We recommend that guests needing special assistance do not select Exit Row seats.

# CEB Baggage Guidelines and Upgrade Options
Bringing home extra pasalubong, or planning out your OOTDs?   If you need to bring more things, you can add CEB Baggage and CEB Special Baggage to your booking. It's available through Manage Booking up to 2 hours before your flight!

## Overview

### Description

## üß≥Checked baggage allowance
Checked baggage allowance is only included in our GO Easy and GO Flexi fare bundles:
| Fare Bundle
| Checked baggage allowance
| GO Basic
| ‚ùå None(Available as Add-on)
| GO Easy
| ‚úÖ 1 piece, 20kg allowance(Size limit: 39x39x39in)
| GO Flexi
For every 20kg of prepaid baggage allowance, you are entitled to bring one (1) piece of checked baggage.

## ‚ûïBaggage Upgrade and Extra Piece Purchase
- If you need toincrease the weight of your 20kg checked baggage, you may upgrade by 4kg, 8kg, or up to 12kg.Please note that upgrading the weight does not change the number of pieces allowed.
- Please note that upgrading the weight does not change the number of pieces allowed.
- If you need toincrease the number of pieces of your checked baggage, you can purchase a maximum of three (3) pieces online, with each piece having a base weight of 20kg.Should you require more than three pieces, additional baggage can be purchased at the airport.This does not apply to flights departingBangkok (BKK)andDon Mueang (DMK), where a temporary baggage policy limits airport purchases to two (2) pieces only.
- Should you require more than three pieces, additional baggage can be purchased at the airport.This does not apply to flights departingBangkok (BKK)andDon Mueang (DMK), where a temporary baggage policy limits airport purchases to two (2) pieces only.
- This does not apply to flights departingBangkok (BKK)andDon Mueang (DMK), where a temporary baggage policy limits airport purchases to two (2) pieces only.
- üí° If you need to bring larger or specialized items, consider gettingCEB Special Baggage Add-on.

## üëú Hand-carry allowance
| Hand-carry allowance
| ‚úÖ 1 piece for overhead binand 1 piece for under the seat, 7kg allowance(Size limit: 22inx 14in x 10in for baggage in the overhead bin and8in x 8in x 14in for baggage under the seat)
- Cabin-size trolley/luggage
- Backpack or laptop/camera bag
- Sling bag, handbag, shoulder bag or small purse
- Items purchased inside the airport, including Duty Free Items (DFI), donuts, fruit boxes, etc.
- Baby bag, medical-related items or food items not accepted for check-in

## Policies & Guides

### Baggage policies
- Small hand-carry¬†under the seat: 8in x 8in x 14in
Any excess in piece, weight, and size are subject to corresponding airport fees, since it will require different handling procedures.These fees vary from airport to airport, so be mindful of size limits!
- Learn more:Airport Baggage Guidelines
For more information about what you can bring on-board or put in your checked baggage, visit the following articles:
- Can I Bring This in My Hand-Carry?
- Can I Bring This in My Checked Baggage?
We aim to make flying convenient and accessible to everyone! If you are:
- üë∂ Traveling with an infant and need to bring a baby stroller/seat/bassinet, or
- üë®‚Äçü¶Ω‚Äç‚û°Ô∏è Traveling with someone who requires a walking cane, wheelchair, or mobility aid,
We are happy to let you know that you can check these in for free!
Note that for battery-powered items, only dry-cell batteries are allowed, and you will be required to remove the batteries before boarding.
For more information about our assistance policies, visit this article:Requesting for Medical, Mobility, and Travel Assistance
Baggage pooling allows guests of the same booking to share their baggage allowance,as long as they check in their bags at the same time.
Baggage pooling only applies to checked baggage and does not include hand-carry items.
üìù Please take note!
- Total Pieces:¬†The combined number of bags must not exceed the number you purchased for check-in.
- Total Weight: The combined weight of all bags must not exceed the total weight¬†you purchased for check-in.
- Maximum Weight: Each checked baggage can weigh up to 32kg.
- To make use of our baggage pooling policy:Make sure to check in your bags with your friends or family at the same time.
- Make sure to check in your bags with your friends or family at the same time.
- The allowance of guests who are not at the airport bag drop counter will not be part of the pooled weight.

### Oversized & special items
üì¶ Transporting human remains and ashes can be done via our CEB Cargo service.Learn more about this service here:Guidelines for Transporting Human Remains
- Household pets, except for snub-nosed breeds, are accepted on flights via our CEB Cargo service only.Learn more about transporting pets in this article:Shipping with Our CEB Cargo Service.
- Learn more about transporting pets in this article:Shipping with Our CEB Cargo Service.
- You may only bring a Service or Emotional Support animal with you in the aircraft.Learn more here:Traveling with Service and Emotional Support Animals
- Learn more here:Traveling with Service and Emotional Support Animals
‚ùóÔ∏èDangerous goods are items or substances that may endanger the society of the aircraft or guests onboard. Please do not pack any items listed here in your hand carry or checked baggage.
The following items are prohibitedin your baggage whether it is checked in or not:
- Explosives, flammable or non-inflammable gas (such as aerosol paints, butane gas, lighter refills)
- Refrigerated gas (such as filled aqualung cylinders, liquid nitrogen)
- Flammable liquids (such as paints, thinners, solvents)
- Flammable solids (such as matches, fire lighters)
- Organic peroxides (such as resins)
- Poisons
- Infective substances (such as viruses, bacteria)
- Radioactive material (such as radium)
- Corrosive materials (such as acid, alkali, mercury, thermometer)
- Magnetic substances, oxidizing materials (such as bleaches)
- Weapons such as antique firearms, swords, knives, and similar items*. Such items may only be allowed in checked baggage at our absolute discretion for very special reasons.
- *For those travelling to/from Hong Kong, please note that stun guns, bullets, extendible batons, and knuckledusters are considered as arms in Hong Kong and therefore are prohibited.

### How to add baggage

## General Guidelines:
- ‚åõ CEB Baggage is available up to two (2) hours before your flight.
- 3Ô∏è‚É£ You can purchase up to three (3) pieces checked baggage (max 32kg per piece).
- üìè The size limit is 39x39x39in.
- üì¶ If you need to bring something larger than this, such as balikbayan boxes, sports equipment, or surfboards, check out this article:CEB Special Baggage Add-on.

However, if you'd like to upgrade your allowance or add another bag, you may do so on the Add-ons page:
| Add-ons Page:
| 1. Tap 'CEB Baggage' on the Add-ons page.
| 2. Choose which flight you want to buy baggage for.If you want to buy baggage for both flights, tap the 'Select for both flights' toggle.
| 3. Choose if you're buying baggage for all passengers, or per passenger.
| 4. Tap the 'Add baggage' button to add a baggage piece (max 3)Each baggage piece has a base allowance of 20kg.

[146] Traveling with Service and Emotional Support Animals
URL      : https://help.cebupacificair.com/article/traveling-with-service-and-emotional-support-animals-121965
CATEGORY : Check-in & Boarding
------------------------------------------------------------
# Traveling with Service and Emotional Support Animals
Cebu Pacific welcomes dogs onboard as either service animals or emotional support animals. No other animals are allowed in the cabin.

## Overview

### Description

## üê∂ What's the difference?
| Type
| Service Dog
| Trained to perform specific tasks for individuals with reduced mobilities (i.e., seeing eye / hearing dog).
| Emotional Support Dog
| Provides comfort and emotional stability to help ease anxiety and depression through companionship. Not task-trained.
General Guidelines:
- Make sure to declare that you'll be bringing your dog with you at the time of booking or via Manage Booking.
- Only one (1) dog is allowed per flight.

## ‚úàÔ∏èAccepted Flights
| Flight
| Service Dogs
| Emotional Support Dogs
| Cebu Pacific (5J)
| ‚úÖ accepted
| Cebgo (DG)
| AirSWIFT (T6)
| ‚ùå not yet accepted; coming soon!
Other household pets may be shipped viaCEB Cargoonly.

## üìã Travel Requirements
| 1.Document confirming the service dog has been trained
| 1.Document with letterhead from your medical doctor supporting the need for emotional support animal
| 2.Complete and up-to-date vaccination card of the dog
| 3. Shipping permit issued by the Bureau of Animal Industry - Department of Agriculture
| 3.Shipping permit issued by the Bureau of Animal Industry - Department of Agriculture

## üêæ Accessories &¬†Setup
- Service Dogs:Must be securelyleashedat all times; not required to wear a mouth-restraint device (i.e., muzzle, mouthguard, mouth cover, collar).
- Emotional Support Dogs:Allowed inside asoft carrierthat fits under the seat (approx. 8in x 8in x 14in).If inside a soft carrier, a leash and mouth-restraint device are not required.If outside a soft carrier, both a leash and a mouth‚Äërestraint device are required.
- If inside a soft carrier, a leash and mouth-restraint device are not required.
- If outside a soft carrier, both a leash and a mouth‚Äërestraint device are required.

## üí∫ Seating Guidelines
- Dogscannot occupy a seator be seated in theexit row.
- Must fit on your lap or within your legroom.
Recommended setup:
- Sit by the window with your dog between you and the window.
If your dog is too large:
- You may be moved to a seat with extra space (if available).
- If the flight is full, you may be rebooked to a later flight to accommodate you and your dog better.
- To guarantee space,purchase an extra seat.Chat with usso we can help you purchase an extra seat.

## üßº Hygiene & Comfort
- Service and emotional support dogs must wearpet diapersand sit onmoisture-absorbing material.
- Alternatively, provide a document stating your dogdoes not need to relieve itselfduring the flight.

## üåé Government Clearances
- All animals imported, transhipped, or exported to/fromSingaporerequire a validAnimal & Veterinary Service (AVS)license.
- For travel to/fromAustralia,refer to this articlefor Seeing Eye dog guidelines.

# Unaccompanied Minor Requirements
Unaccompanied Minors are guests aged 7 to below 12 years old at the time of travel. Learn more about the requirements and crucial reminders for minors traveling alone.

## Overview

### Description
- 7 to 11 years old at the time of travel;
- Traveling alone without an adult companion who is at least 18 years old; and
- Traveling within the Philippines.
- Children below 7 years old:They won't be allowed to board without an adult companion who is at least 18 years old.
- Minors aged 12 and above: They are considered adult guests, and do not require the UM Service.
- Minors on international flights: They won't be allowed to board without an adult companion who is¬†at least 18 years old.
This service is provided to ensure the child‚Äôs safety and comfort during the flight. The cost of Unaccompanied Minor Fee is indicated when you book your flight.

## üìù General Guidelines
To avail of the UM Service, the parent/guardian must:
- Complete the Passenger Handling Form.Please fill this out at least 24 hours before your flight.
- Please fill this out at least 24 hours before your flight.
- Pay for the Unaccompanied Minor Fee;
- Endorse the child at the check-in counter.Please present their valid ID, along with the child's travel documents;
- Please present their valid ID, along with the child's travel documents;
- Stay at the airport until the child's flight has departed.
Important Reminders:
- The UM Service is only available on domestic flights.
- The UM Service is not available for minors who need Portable Oxygen Concentrators (POC)For their safety, they must travel with an adult companion who is at least 18 years old.
- For their safety, they must travel with an adult companion who is at least 18 years old.
- We can only accept a limited number of unaccompanied minors per flight.Make sure you set them as "Children" when you first book your flight.
- Make sure you set them as "Children" when you first book your flight.
üìùFilipino minors (under 18) need a travel clearancefrom the Department of Social Welfare and Development (DSWD) if they are:
- Traveling internationally alone, or
- Traveling internationally with someone other than their parents or legal guardian.
This permit states that it is with full knowledge of the parents that the child is travelling out of the country.
- To apply for travel clearance, use DSWD‚ÄôsMinors Traveling Abroad System. Walk-in applications will not be entertained.
- For online application guidance, watch thisvideo.
For minors with foreign nationalities,please check the rules governing minor travel as issued by your respective governments.

## ‚úàÔ∏è Traveling to and from Davao City
- They are traveling alone, or
- Traveling with a person other than their parents/legal guardians.
Below are the required documents for the permit to travel:
Bi. Birth Certificate of the minor (original and photocopy)
Ba. Barangay Clearance issued by the Punong Barangay, stating that the barangay has knowledge of the travel plans of the minor
Wr. Written parental consent attested by the Punong Barangay (if no parents, consent shall be made by the grandparents or eldest¬†sibling)
Id. Identification Card of the minor (original and photocopy)
Id. Identification Card of the authorized person who will accompany the child in his travels (original and photocopy).
If a child/minor is traveling with both or any of their parents,there is no need to secure a permitas long as there is a document to¬†prove the minor's relations such as:
Bi. Birth Certificate
Va. Valid IDs

## üìù Other Info
- If you need to rebook an unaccompanied minor's flight, you won't have to pay for the UM fee again.
- If you made a separate booking for a Child guest, but you will be traveling on the same flight as them:Chat with us via app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can refund the UM Fee.

[152] Bangkok (Suvarnabhumi) Airport and Travel Guide

------------------------------------------------------------
# Bangkok (Suvarnabhumi) Airport and Travel Guide
Plan your trip with this Bangkok Suvarnabhumi Airport travel guide, featuring Thailand's entry requirements, airport facilities, and essential travel tips.

## Overview

### Description
‚úàÔ∏è Cebu Pacific operates flights on theManila-Bangkok-Manilaroute twice daily via Ninoy Aquino International Airport Terminal 3, and on theClark-Bangkok-Clarkroute ten times weekly via Clark International Airport. All flights arrive at and depart from the Main Terminal of Bangkok Suvarnabhumi Airport (BKK).
Bangkok Suvarnabhumi Airport (BKK) is one of the busiest airports in Southeast Asia, serving as a major hub for international and domestic flights. It operates as asilent airport, meaning there are minimal public announcements to reduce noise pollution and create a more peaceful environment for travelers. Passengers are encouraged to rely on the flight information display screens (FIDS) located throughout the airport for updates on flight status, boarding gates, and other important information.

## Guide & Travel Requirements

### General Guidelines
Passport and visa
- Make sure your passport is valid for at least six months from your date of entry and has at least one blank page.
- Philippine passport holders can enter Thailand without a visa for stays no longer than 60 days.
- For non-Philippine passport holders, please check here if you'll need a visa:Cebu Pacific TravelDoc
Thailand Digital Arrival Card (TDAC)
- The TDAC is an online form that replaces the traditional paper-based arrival card for international travelers entering Thailand. This is free of charge and can be submitted within 3 days before entering Thailand.
- VisitThailand Digital Arrival Card (TDAC) articleto learn more.
- Followthe signs to the immigration counters and be prepared for possible random security checks.
- Present your passport and visa (if applicable) at the immigration counters.
- Travelers are encouraged to carry a digital or printed copy of the TDAC confirmation for reference upon arrival.
Claiming Baggage:
- After immigration, proceed to claim your baggage at the baggage claim area.
- Check the respective baggage carousel on the display screen for your flight.
- For any lost and found concerns, please emailbaggage.services@airportthai.co.th
- Use the green lane if you have nothing to declare, or the red lane if you have items to declare.
- For more information about Thailand's customs procedure for arriving passengers, visitThai Customs.
Philippine e-Travel Form:
- Anyone entering the Philippines, including guests on layover flights, must register for theeTraveland Customs Declarationwithin 72 hours before their flight.
- eTravel declaration is free of charge and is mandatory for travel to the Philippines.
- Arrive at the airport at least three (3) hours before your flight.Our airport counters close one (1) hour before departure.
- Our airport counters close one (1) hour before departure.
- Check the display screens to¬†find information aboutthe counters for your flight.
- Prepare your valid passport, booking confirmation or Itinerary Receipt, and visa (if applicable) for checking at the counters.
- Makeyour airport experience smoother and quicker by using Cebu Pacific‚Äôs self-service kiosks for check-in and bag tag printing. Simply prepare your booking reference number or barcode to retrieve your booking.
- Ifyou checked in online, a digital boarding pass is accepted when departing from Bangkok (Suvarnabhumi).
- Make sure to keep in mind your booking's baggage allowance.Learn more here:CEB Baggage Guidelines and Upgrade Options
- Learn more here:CEB Baggage Guidelines and Upgrade Options
Customs & Boarding:
- Check your printed boarding pass and the nearest display screen to find the boarding gate number.
Passenger Rights:
- You have certain rights as an air passenger in case of flight disruptions.
- For more information, please visit the following articles:How to Manage Your Disrupted FlightDelays and Cancelations at the AirportPassenger Rights & Airline Policies
- How to Manage Your Disrupted Flight
- Delays and Cancelations at the Airport
- Passenger Rights & Airline Policies
- AtBangkok (Suvarnabhumi)International Airport, communication with passengers is primarily done through flight information display screens (FIDS) and printed or digital signages.
- We also encourage passengers to monitor their email for important updates from Cebu Pacific.
Exiting the airport:
- If your flight is disrupted afterimmigration and customs clearance, you may be allowed to exitBangkok (Suvarnabhumi)International Airport. In such cases, you will need to surrender your passport to immigration officers. Duty-free items can be brought out of the airport as well.

# Transfer of Cebgo (DG) and AirSWIFT (T6) Flights from Manila to Clark
Starting March 29, 2026, Cebgo (DG) and AirSWIFT (T6) flights will depart and arrive in Clark International Airport.

## Overview

### Description
StartingMarch 29, 2026, all Cebgo (DG) and AirSWIFT (T6) flights will transfer from Ninoy Aquino International Airport (MNL) toClark International Airport (CRK).This change is in line with the resolution from the Department of Transportation'sManila Slot Coordination Committee, which requires the complete transfer of turboprop aircraft operations from MNL to CRK. This is part of efforts to enhance overall passenger experience.

## FAQ

### General Guidelines
The transfer of allCebgo (DG) and AirSWIFT (T6) flightsfrom Ninoy Aquino International Airport (MNL) to Clark International Airport (CRK) will begin onMarch 29, 2026.
This change is in line with the resolution from the Department of Transportation'sManila Slot Coordination Committee, which requires the transfer of turboprop aircraft operations from NAIA (MNL) to Clark International Airport (CRK).This is part of efforts to enhance overall passenger experience.

### Other Concerns
You will still be departing from NAIA Terminal 2 (MNL), and you will be arriving at Clark International Airport (CRK).

- ‚è≥ You can only make this change within 24 hours from the time of booking completion;
- ‚òùÔ∏èYou can only update this once.
If it's more than 24 hours since you made your booking:
- üí¨ Pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can validate your request;
- üìÑ Please prepare proof of the name correction, e.g., marriage certificate, or other supporting documents.
Special characters in your name:
- If your name has special characters (e.g., √±, √©, √º) please replace them with the regular letter instead (e.g., Ni√±a ‚û°Ô∏è Nina).
- For names with apostrophes or hyphens, you may replace them with a space (e.g., Mary-Jane‚û°Ô∏è Mary Jane, O'Connor ‚û°Ô∏è O Connor).
- If your boarding pass or itinerary shows your name without special characters, don't worry! Your booking is still valid.
Suffixes in your name:
- If your name has a suffix (Jr., Sr., III), proceed to enter the suffix in the "First Name" field.
- Enter your name exactly as it is shown in your valid ID.
General Guidelines:
- üë§ An account is required to make any booking changes.
- ‚ùå Booking isNOTtransferable to another guest.

## ‚úíÔ∏èUpdate Nationality/Passport, Birthday, Salutation, or Contact Number
You can update these details up to 2 hours before your flight, via Manage Booking.
- ‚è≥ This is only available up to 2 hours before your flight;
- ‚òùÔ∏è For nationality/passport, birthday, and salutation details, you can only update this once.
- ‚úåÔ∏è For your contact number, you can update this multiple times as necessary.
- Please approach the airport counters for assistance.
For OFWs, you can change or add your Overseas Employment Certificate (OEC) / MIAA Exemption Certificate (MEC) number even after completion of booking through the following channels:
- Chat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can validate your request.
- If you're at the airport, please approach theOverseas Workers Welfare Administration (OWWA) counter.
- Once you're at the counter, present any of these documents, OEC issued by the OWWA; OEC Balik Manggagawa Certificate; or MEC.

## üì© Update Email Address
- üí¨ If you wish to change your email address, pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help.

# Traveling with Infants or Minors
Learn about age-specific travel rules, seat options, and required documents for infants and minors flying with Cebu Pacific to ensure a safe and smooth journey.

## Overview

### Description

## üë∂ Infant or below 2 years old
AnInfant Feewill be applied to guests traveling with an infant due to the special assistance required. Guests have the following options:
- Infant without seat:The infant will sit on the adult's lap.No baggage allowance will be given for infants on lap.
- The infant will sit on the adult's lap.
- No baggage allowance will be given for infants on lap.
- Infant with seat:The infant will occupy their own seat next to the parent/guardian's‚Äîcharged at the lowest available fare.The infant will have their own hand-carry baggage allowance. They can also purchase up to three (3) pieces of checked baggage.Infants with seat are required to have a Child Restraint System (CRS) that conforms to Federal Motor Vehicle Safety Standards (FMVSS) or certified by the Civil Aviation Authority (CAA).
- The infant will occupy their own seat next to the parent/guardian's‚Äîcharged at the lowest available fare.
- The infant will have their own hand-carry baggage allowance. They can also purchase up to three (3) pieces of checked baggage.
- Infants with seat are required to have a Child Restraint System (CRS) that conforms to Federal Motor Vehicle Safety Standards (FMVSS) or certified by the Civil Aviation Authority (CAA).
- For their safety, infants below 8 days old will not be accepted for carriage.
- Infants can only travel if accompanied by an adult aged 18 years and above. Only one (1) infant is allowed per adult passenger.
- Guests traveling with infants may present the infant's physical passport, birth certificate, or baby book as identification during check-in.

## üë∂Ages 2 to 6 years
Children below 7 years old are not allowed to travel alone. They may only be accepted if they are accompanied by a person at least 18 years old.

- Parents or guardians may be asked to submit additional identity verification at the check-in counter.

Va. Valid IDs

- Accomplished Unaccompanied Minor Form and paid Unaccompanied Minor Handling Fee
- ID of a parent/guardian accompanying the minor on departure
- ID of parent/guardian picking up the minor on arrival
- ID of traveling child
- Paid Unaccompanied Minor Handling Fee
- Confirmed flight segments
Learn more here:Unaccompanied Minor Requirements

## üë∂Ages 12 to 17 years
Young passengers aged 12 to 17 years are allowed to travel alone.
- Passengers below 18 years old traveling from Davaomust present Travel Permit issued by the City Social Welfare and Development Office (CSWDO)¬† or by the Special Office for Children's Concerns (SOCC) at check-in.
- Filipino passengers aged 12 to 17 yearstraveling alone to international destinationsmust present Travel Clearance issued by the Department of Social Welfare and Development (DSWD).
- Foreign passengers below 15 years old entering the Philippinesmust secure a Waiver of Exclusion Ground (WEG) from the Bureau of Immigration.

# Cebu Pacific International Travel Guide
Ready for your next flight? This guide offers significant departure and arrival details for Cebu Pacific international destinations.

## Overview

### Description
If you're carrying more thanPHP 50,000 or USD 10,000(or equivalent in other currencies), you need to:
- Declare the amount when filling your eTravel details
- For PH currency, secure authorization from the Bangko Sentral ng Pilipinas
Non-declaration or false declaration shall be subject to confiscation and/or legal action.
Before arriving at the airport, make sure to check in online!
If you can't check in online, you can line up at the regular airport counters.
‚úàÔ∏èFor international flights,airport counters close one (1) hour before departure.Please arrive at the airport three (3) hours before your flight schedule.

------------------------------------------------------------
# Traveling with Service and Emotional Support Animals
Cebu Pacific welcomes dogs onboard as either service animals or emotional support animals. No other animals are allowed in the cabin.

## Overview

### Description

## üê∂ What's the difference?
| Type
| Service Dog
| Trained to perform specific tasks for individuals with reduced mobilities (i.e., seeing eye / hearing dog).
| Emotional Support Dog
| Provides comfort and emotional stability to help ease anxiety and depression through companionship. Not task-trained.
General Guidelines:
- Make sure to declare that you'll be bringing your dog with you at the time of booking or via Manage Booking.
- Only one (1) dog is allowed per flight.

## ‚úàÔ∏èAccepted Flights
| Flight
| Service Dogs
| Emotional Support Dogs
| Cebu Pacific (5J)
| ‚úÖ accepted
| Cebgo (DG)
| AirSWIFT (T6)
| ‚ùå not yet accepted; coming soon!
Other household pets may be shipped viaCEB Cargoonly.

## üìã Travel Requirements
| 1.Document confirming the service dog has been trained
| 1.Document with letterhead from your medical doctor supporting the need for emotional support animal
| 2.Complete and up-to-date vaccination card of the dog
| 3. Shipping permit issued by the Bureau of Animal Industry - Department of Agriculture
| 3.Shipping permit issued by the Bureau of Animal Industry - Department of Agriculture

## üêæ Accessories &¬†Setup
- Service Dogs:Must be securelyleashedat all times; not required to wear a mouth-restraint device (i.e., muzzle, mouthguard, mouth cover, collar).
- Emotional Support Dogs:Allowed inside asoft carrierthat fits under the seat (approx. 8in x 8in x 14in).If inside a soft carrier, a leash and mouth-restraint device are not required.If outside a soft carrier, both a leash and a mouth‚Äërestraint device are required.
- If inside a soft carrier, a leash and mouth-restraint device are not required.
- If outside a soft carrier, both a leash and a mouth‚Äërestraint device are required.

## üí∫ Seating Guidelines
- Dogscannot occupy a seator be seated in theexit row.
- Must fit on your lap or within your legroom.
Recommended setup:
- Sit by the window with your dog between you and the window.
If your dog is too large:
- You may be moved to a seat with extra space (if available).
- If the flight is full, you may be rebooked to a later flight to accommodate you and your dog better.
- To guarantee space,purchase an extra seat.Chat with usso we can help you purchase an extra seat.

## üßº Hygiene & Comfort
- Service and emotional support dogs must wearpet diapersand sit onmoisture-absorbing material.
- Alternatively, provide a document stating your dogdoes not need to relieve itselfduring the flight.

## üåé Government Clearances
- All animals imported, transhipped, or exported to/fromSingaporerequire a validAnimal & Veterinary Service (AVS)license.
- For travel to/fromAustralia,refer to this articlefor Seeing Eye dog guidelines.

[173] Philippine eTravel System
URL      : https://help.cebupacificair.com/article/philippine-e-travel-system-198094
CATEGORY : Prepare for Your Flight
------------------------------------------------------------
# Philippine eTravel System
Planning to travel abroad? Learn how the Philippine eTravel System makes your journey smoother!

## Overview

### Description
TheeTravel Systemis a web-based platform developed by the Philippine government to simplify and digitize travel documentation for international travelers. It serves as a one-stop portal that consolidates health declarations (via the Bureau of Quarantine), immigration clearance (via the Bureau of Immigration), customs declarations, and travel tax declaration and payment (via TIEZA). Accessible throughetravel.gov.ph, the system is also integrated into theeGovPH app, making it easier for travelers to manage their requirements in one place.
All passengers entering the Philippines‚Äîincluding Philippine passport holders, foreign nationals, and airline crew‚Äîas well as all Filipino passengers departing from the Philippines, are required by the government to complete thee-Travel form. This requirement applies to bothleisure and business travel.
Registration must be completedwithin 72 hours (3 days)before your scheduled arrival or departure. You can register from home or at the airport before check-in, but it‚Äôs highly recommended to do it in advance to avoid delays.

## FAQ

### General Guidelines

### Travel Tax Payment and Declaration

### Customs Declaration

### Health Declaration

# How to Manage Your Disrupted Flight
Manage disrupted flights anywhere ‚Äî no need to visit the airport!

## Overview

### Description

## General Guidelines
While we continuously work to ensure your flight departs and arrives on time, on-the-spot delays or cancelations may occur due to environmental, operational or technical reasons.
- Affected passengers will be notified by Cebu Pacific frontline team, email, and/or text message.
- You can check the real-time status of your flight through ourFlight Status page.
- We will ensure your welfare is taken care of whenever there are planned or on-the-spot changes to flights.Know your rights as an air passenger through this article:Passenger Rights & Airline PoliciesCheck the applicable options for on-the-spot disruptions:Disruptions at the airport
- Know your rights as an air passenger through this article:Passenger Rights & Airline Policies
- Passenger Rights & Airline Policies
- Check the applicable options for on-the-spot disruptions:Disruptions at the airport
- Disruptions at the airport
After being notified of the disruption, you will be given a link to our Self-Service Disruption Portal (SSDP).
You may also access this by going toManage Bookingon the Cebu Pacific app or website.

## üìù Disruption options
We offer the following flexible options for disrupted guests:
- Rebook your flightRebook your flight for free up to 30 days before or 30 days after your original schedule.If you need to rebook beyond the 30-day period,pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help.
Rebook your flight
- Rebook your flight for free up to 30 days before or 30 days after your original schedule.
- If you need to rebook beyond the 30-day period,pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help.
- Request a refundRequest a refund of your fare according to your form of payment.Travel Tax and unused TravelSure will have to be refunded separately.Learn more here:Refund Concerns
Request a refund
- Request a refund of your fare according to your form of payment.
- Travel Tax and unused TravelSure will have to be refunded separately.
- Learn more here:Refund Concerns
- Convert to Travel FundWhen converting your disrupted flight to Travel Fund, it¬†will be stored in yourbooking reference number.With this, you can use it to pay for future flights or add-ons.Once you reach the payment page, simply enter thesix-digit booking reference numberthat contains the Travel Fund.Learn more about the Travel Fund here:CEB Flexi & Travel Fund
Convert to Travel Fund
- When converting your disrupted flight to Travel Fund, it¬†will be stored in yourbooking reference number.
- With this, you can use it to pay for future flights or add-ons.
- Once you reach the payment page, simply enter thesix-digit booking reference numberthat contains the Travel Fund.
- Learn more about the Travel Fund here:CEB Flexi & Travel Fund
- üí°Remember!Once you pick an option, it's final and can't be changed or undone.You can only rebook, refund, or convert your disrupted flight to Travel Fundonce.When rebooking, make sure you're selecting the correct flight dates!
- Once you pick an option, it's final and can't be changed or undone.
- You can only rebook, refund, or convert your disrupted flight to Travel Fundonce.
- When rebooking, make sure you're selecting the correct flight dates!

------------------------------------------------------------
# CEB Flexi and Travel Fund
Book your flight with CEB Flexi for more savings and flexibility in your travel plans. Cancel your flight for FREE and convert the value of your booking to a Travel Fund!

## Overview

### Description

## üìÜ CEB Flexi
Change of plans? No problem. With CEB Flexi, you can cancel your trip for free.
It allows you to cancel your booking and convert its value to a non-expiring Travel Fund.
- Cancelation is available up to two (2) hours before departure
- You can then use this Travel Fund to pay for your future travel plans!
Once you convert to Travel Fund, it will appear in your account within 24 hours.
General Guidelines:
- CEB Flexi only allows for free cancellation;It does not cover rebooking change fees.
- It does not cover rebooking change fees.
- You cannot add CEB Flexi after you've finished booking your flight;
- The price of CEB Flexi is based on your flight date, and on regulatory guidelines.
- If you purchased CEB Flexi without a MyCebuPacific account, and you intend to cancel your flight later on:Pleasesign up or log into your MyCebuPacific account first.Remember!An account is required to make booking changes.Check out ourhow-to guidesto know how to voluntarily cancel your flight and convert it to Travel Fund with CEB Flexi.
- Pleasesign up or log into your MyCebuPacific account first.
- Remember!An account is required to make booking changes.
- Check out ourhow-to guidesto know how to voluntarily cancel your flight and convert it to Travel Fund with CEB Flexi.

## ü™ô Travel Fund
Travel Fund is a non-expiring virtual wallet that you can use to pay for your future trips. It's available if:
- You purchased CEB Flexi and used it to cancel your flight, or;
- Your flight was disrupted (i.e. canceled or had a 1hr+ schedule change).How to Manage Your Disrupted Flight
- How to Manage Your Disrupted Flight
- Guest/s in the booking has a serious illness, or has died;Guest's immediate family member has died.
- Guest's immediate family member has died.
- AMyCebuPacific Accountis required to make booking changes;
- Once you convert to Travel Fund, it will appear in your MyCebuPacific account within 24 hours;
- The currency of your Travel Fund will depend on what currency you used when booking your flight.
- The Travel Fund can be split among guests in the same booking.With this, pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help you.
- With this, pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help you.
- ‚ùå The Travel Fund cannot be exchanged or converted to cash.
When you convert a booking to Travel Fund, it includes:
- Fares and taxes;
- All unused add-ons
- Admin and handling fees.
Conversion to Travel Fund does not include:
- Travel taxas this is refunded separately;
- Cost of CEB Flexi;
- Cost ofCEB TravelSure insuranceas this is refunded separately;
- Flight fees, such as the hold fee and cancel fee (if applicable).

# Updating Your Guest or Contact Details
Made a typo? You can go to Manage Booking within 24 hours of booking to change either your First or your Last Name! You can also update your other contact and guest details up to 2 hours before your flight.

## Overview

### Description

## ‚úèÔ∏èUpdate Name
- ‚ö†Ô∏è You can update either yourFirst Name only, or yourLast Name only;
- ‚è≥ You can only make this change within 24 hours from the time of booking completion;
- ‚òùÔ∏èYou can only update this once.
If it's more than 24 hours since you made your booking:
- üí¨ Pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can validate your request;
- üìÑ Please prepare proof of the name correction, e.g., marriage certificate, or other supporting documents.
Special characters in your name:
- If your name has special characters (e.g., √±, √©, √º) please replace them with the regular letter instead (e.g., Ni√±a ‚û°Ô∏è Nina).
- For names with apostrophes or hyphens, you may replace them with a space (e.g., Mary-Jane‚û°Ô∏è Mary Jane, O'Connor ‚û°Ô∏è O Connor).
- If your boarding pass or itinerary shows your name without special characters, don't worry! Your booking is still valid.
Suffixes in your name:
- If your name has a suffix (Jr., Sr., III), proceed to enter the suffix in the "First Name" field.
- Enter your name exactly as it is shown in your valid ID.
General Guidelines:
- üë§ An account is required to make any booking changes.
- ‚ùå Booking isNOTtransferable to another guest.

## ‚úíÔ∏èUpdate Nationality/Passport, Birthday, Salutation, or Contact Number
You can update these details up to 2 hours before your flight, via Manage Booking.
- ‚è≥ This is only available up to 2 hours before your flight;
- ‚òùÔ∏è For nationality/passport, birthday, and salutation details, you can only update this once.
- ‚úåÔ∏è For your contact number, you can update this multiple times as necessary.
- Please approach the airport counters for assistance.
For OFWs, you can change or add your Overseas Employment Certificate (OEC) / MIAA Exemption Certificate (MEC) number even after completion of booking through the following channels:
- Chat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can validate your request.
- If you're at the airport, please approach theOverseas Workers Welfare Administration (OWWA) counter.
- Once you're at the counter, present any of these documents, OEC issued by the OWWA; OEC Balik Manggagawa Certificate; or MEC.

## üì© Update Email Address
- üí¨ If you wish to change your email address, pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help.

[198] CEB Flexi and Travel Fund
URL      : https://help.cebupacificair.com/article/ceb-flexi-and-travel-fund-123947
CATEGORY : Suspension of Cebu Pacific Flights Between Cebu and San Vicente
------------------------------------------------------------
# CEB Flexi and Travel Fund
Book your flight with CEB Flexi for more savings and flexibility in your travel plans. Cancel your flight for FREE and convert the value of your booking to a Travel Fund!

## Overview

### Description

## üìÜ CEB Flexi
Change of plans? No problem. With CEB Flexi, you can cancel your trip for free.
It allows you to cancel your booking and convert its value to a non-expiring Travel Fund.
- Cancelation is available up to two (2) hours before departure
- You can then use this Travel Fund to pay for your future travel plans!
Once you convert to Travel Fund, it will appear in your account within 24 hours.
General Guidelines:
- CEB Flexi only allows for free cancellation;It does not cover rebooking change fees.
- It does not cover rebooking change fees.
- You cannot add CEB Flexi after you've finished booking your flight;
- The price of CEB Flexi is based on your flight date, and on regulatory guidelines.
- If you purchased CEB Flexi without a MyCebuPacific account, and you intend to cancel your flight later on:Pleasesign up or log into your MyCebuPacific account first.Remember!An account is required to make booking changes.Check out ourhow-to guidesto know how to voluntarily cancel your flight and convert it to Travel Fund with CEB Flexi.
- Pleasesign up or log into your MyCebuPacific account first.
- Remember!An account is required to make booking changes.
- Check out ourhow-to guidesto know how to voluntarily cancel your flight and convert it to Travel Fund with CEB Flexi.

## ü™ô Travel Fund
Travel Fund is a non-expiring virtual wallet that you can use to pay for your future trips. It's available if:
- You purchased CEB Flexi and used it to cancel your flight, or;
- Your flight was disrupted (i.e. canceled or had a 1hr+ schedule change).How to Manage Your Disrupted Flight
- How to Manage Your Disrupted Flight
- Guest/s in the booking has a serious illness, or has died;Guest's immediate family member has died.
- Guest's immediate family member has died.
- AMyCebuPacific Accountis required to make booking changes;
- Once you convert to Travel Fund, it will appear in your MyCebuPacific account within 24 hours;
- The currency of your Travel Fund will depend on what currency you used when booking your flight.
- The Travel Fund can be split among guests in the same booking.With this, pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help you.
- With this, pleasechat with usvia our app or website to connect with a Live Agent who can help you.
- ‚ùå The Travel Fund cannot be exchanged or converted to cash.
When you convert a booking to Travel Fund, it includes:
- Fares and taxes;
- All unused add-ons
- Admin and handling fees.
Conversion to Travel Fund does not include:
- Travel taxas this is refunded separately;
- Cost of CEB Flexi;
- Cost ofCEB TravelSure insuranceas this is refunded separately;
- Flight fees, such as the hold fee and cancel fee (if applicable).

# How to Earn and Redeem Go Rewards Points
You can earn Go Rewards points every time you book a flight or buy add-ons online. You can then use those same points to pay for future flights!

## Overview

### Description
Earn Go Rewards points when you book a flight or buy the following add-ons:
- Seats
- Baggage
- Meals
